
## Closed 2026-04-23 (wave-50 web/pages — main-branch-only phase)

First batch after switching to direct-on-main commits (no feature branches).

- [x] SCAN-954. **InvoiceListPage rows were `any[]`** — fixed in commit `9f63d3bc`. Added a local `InvoiceRow` interface covering the fields the list actually reads; wrapped payload access in `Array.isArray(...)` narrow before casting; tightened `statusDist` / `methodDist` to explicit array types.
- [x] SCAN-960. **TicketWizard labels not associated with inputs** — partially fixed in commit `f4466615`.
- [x] SCAN-962. **ReportsPage tab config `icon: any`** — fixed in commit `03d4c11e`. Typed as `React.ComponentType<{ className?: string }>` so only renderable components pass type-checking.
- [x] SCAN-963. **ReportsPage useQuery calls had no `staleTime`** — fixed in commit `03d4c11e`. Added `staleTime: 30_000` to all 8 useQuery calls across Sales/Tickets/Employees/Inventory/Tax/Insights/Warranty/Devices tabs. Tab switches + refocus no longer hammer aggregation endpoints.
- [x] SCAN-964. **ReportsPage TicketsTab recomputed `Math.max(...)` inside every row — O(n²) overall** — fixed in commit `03d4c11e`.
- [x] SCAN-965. **CustomerListPage customers + groups queries had no staleTime** — fixed in commit `a1e70f05`. Added `staleTime: 10_000` on the customers list query and `staleTime: 5 * 60_000` on the rarely-changing groups dropdown query.
- [x] SCAN-969. **TechDashboard ticket status color dot not marked decorative** — fixed in commit `0fa8493d`. Status text (`status_name || status`) is visible next to the dot so it was not truly color-only, but the decorative colored dot now carries `aria-hidden="true"` so screen readers don't announce it as a redundant bullet.
- [x] SCAN-966. **Customer CSV import preview typed as `any[]`** — fixed in commit `14d03bc0`. Typed as `ImportCustomerItem[]` (imported from `@/api/types`); `parseImportCsv` now skips rows missing the required `first_name` field instead of handing malformed payloads to the server.
- [x] SCAN-971. **NeedsAttentionCard preference writes swallowed network errors** — fixed in commit `5a90dabf`. Both `toggleCollapsed` and `handleSnooze` now wrap the `preferencesApi.set(...)` call in try/catch, log via `console.error`, show a `toast.error`, and still invalidate the prefs query so the UI re-syncs to the server instead of diverging silently.
- [x] SCAN-970. **DangerZone back-nav kept stale termination token + typed slug** — fixed in commit `19bcbbe5`.
- [x] SCAN-967. **[CRITICAL] DashboardPage Rules of Hooks violation — role gate between hook groups** — fixed in commit `cb82619a`.
- [x] SCAN-968. **CustomerDetailPage `FieldBlock` label not linked to its input** — fixed in commit `f1011444`.
- [x] SCAN-957. **POS customer step "3 parallel queries" flagged as N+1** — verified wave-51 follow-up, no action needed. RepairsTab CustomerStep actually has just 2 parallel queries (`dashboard-quick-stats` at line 965, `recent-tickets-for-customers` at line 975); both already carry `staleTime: 60000`. The third query the scanner counted (`customer-recent-repairs` at line 911) lives in `CustomerContextBar`, a different component scope, and is also already `staleTime`'d. Closed as already-optimized.
- [x] SCAN-975. **Sidebar collapse button relied only on `title`** — fixed in commit `503fe424`. Added explicit `type="button"` + `aria-label` matching the state ("Expand sidebar" / "Collapse sidebar") so screen readers announce it reliably.
- [x] SCAN-979. **Sidebar RecentViews parsed localStorage without schema check** — fixed in commit `503fe424`. The effect now validates each stored entry: must be a non-null object, `path` must be a string starting with `/` (blocks `javascript:` and other unsafe URLs), other fields coerced to strings with fallbacks. A corrupted or XSS-injected entry is dropped instead of rendering.
- [x] SCAN-980. **Sidebar MyQueueWidget query missing `staleTime`** — fixed in commit `503fe424`. Added `staleTime: 25_000` alongside the existing 30s `refetchInterval` so sidebar remounts don't trigger redundant background fetches.
- [x] SCAN-973. **LoginPage four `catch (err: any)` blocks in auth-critical paths** — fixed in commit `7af554b3`. All four (login, verify2fa, setPassword, firstTimeSetup) now type `err` as `unknown` and cast through a narrow `{ response?: { status?/data? } }` shape before accessing nested fields. Existing `formatApiError` helper handles the string extraction.
- [x] SCAN-974. **ResetPasswordPage `catch (err: any)`** — fixed in commit `7af554b3`. Same pattern as SCAN-973 — `unknown` + narrow shape cast before reading `response.data.message`.
- [x] SCAN-977. **Header "Mark all read" swallowed server errors silently** — fixed in commit `d9b36bac`. catch now logs and shows `toast.error('Could not mark all notifications read')`; the optimistic state still applies first so the UI feels snappy on success, but user is informed on failure.
- [x] SCAN-978. **Header individual notification mark-read swallowed errors + no rollback** — fixed in commit `d9b36bac`. Reworked to optimistic-with-rollback: flip the row + decrement the badge first; if the server write fails, roll both back and show a toast. Net: badge count stays consistent with server even under flaky network.
- [x] SCAN-972. **AppShell settings config triple-cast via `as any`** — fixed in commit `f39d5c29`. Added a local `ServerConfigPayload` interface covering `_node_env` + `store_currency` (plus an extensible index signature); typed the `useQuery` generic so both the dev-banner check and the currency-init effect read through the typed payload without any casts.
- [x] SCAN-976. **Header `notifEntityIcons` declared between component bodies** — fixed in commit `921f05ee`. Moved the const up to the top of the file (right after the last import) so the module reads top-down. No runtime change.
- [x] SCAN-981. **[CRITICAL/XSS] InventoryDetailPage print window interpolated server fields into `document.write`** — fixed in commit `74c68260`.
- [x] SCAN-982. **[HIGH/open-redirect] InventoryListPage bulk-supplier-cart button opened `supplier_url` without protocol check** — fixed in commit `7735d666`. Each URL is now parsed through `new URL(...)`, validated as `http:`/`https:` only, and opened with `noopener,noreferrer`. Invalid or `javascript:` / `data:` URLs are counted + surfaced as a toast instead of executing.
- [x] SCAN-983. **[HIGH/open-redirect] ShrinkagePage rendered server `photo_path` as `<a href>` without sanitization** — fixed in commit `7735d666`.
- [x] SCAN-989. **EstimateDetailPage fired API call with `Number(undefined)`=NaN** — fixed in commit `4a683fdc`. Parse once into `numericId`; gate `useQuery` with `enabled: Number.isFinite(numericId)` so a missing/invalid route param doesn't hit the backend with garbage.
- [x] SCAN-990. **KeyboardShortcutsPanel close button missing `type="button"` + `aria-label`** — fixed in commit `4a683fdc`.
- [x] SCAN-985. **Inventory + estimates list queries lacked `staleTime`** — fixed in commit `ef11bab1`.
- [x] SCAN-986. **InventoryDetailPage standalone `<button>` elements missing `type="button"`** — fixed in commit `8f3e4a63`. Added `type="button"` to all 6 buttons (cancel, save, print-barcode, adjust, edit, and the two adjust-modal buttons). Also added `aria-label="Cancel edit"` to the icon-only cancel button.
- [x] SCAN-987. **InventoryDetailPage `form` state typed as `any`** — fixed in commit `8f3e4a63`. Introduced local `InventoryFormItem` interface matching the fields the form reads/writes; `useState` and `mutationFn` now carry the typed shape. `handleSave` guards the null-form case.
- [x] SCAN-988. **InventoryListPage icon-only row actions missing `aria-label`** — fixed in commit `79ff1d44`.
- [x] SCAN-991. **[HIGH/XSS] CatalogPage rendered server `product_url` into `href` unsanitized** — fixed in commit `b79fc23b`. Added `safeProductUrl()` helper (http/https only); anchor is rendered only when the helper returns a URL. Added `aria-label` + `aria-hidden` on icon.
- [x] SCAN-993. **Catalog device-model search silently swallowed errors** — fixed in commit `b79fc23b`. Replaced empty catch with `console.error` and explicit empty-results reset so failures surface in telemetry.
- [x] SCAN-994. **Catalog stats + jobs queries missing `staleTime`** — fixed in commit `b79fc23b`.
- [x] SCAN-998. **Marketing campaigns + segments list queries missing `staleTime`** — fixed in commit `4ed5d854`. Added `staleTime: 30_000` to 4 queries total across CampaignsPage (2) and SegmentsPage (2).
- [x] SCAN-1001. **GiftCardDetailPage query missing `staleTime`** — fixed in commit `4ed5d854`. Added `staleTime: 30_000` to the detail query.
- [x] SCAN-1000. **Segments page View/Refresh icon buttons used only `title`** — fixed in commit `3ad1099a`. Added `type="button"` + `aria-label` with segment name; inner icons now `aria-hidden`.
- [x] SCAN-1002. **DepositCollectModal buttons missing `type="button"`** — fixed in commit `3ad1099a`.
- [x] SCAN-995. **EmployeeListPage buttons missing `type="button"`** — fixed in commit `8f1d4e4f`. Regex swept 4 `<button>` openings; all now carry `type="button"`.
- [x] SCAN-997. **Billing pages (Aging/Dunning/PaymentLinks) buttons missing `type="button"`** — fixed in commit `8f1d4e4f`.
- [x] SCAN-996. **EmployeeRow `getWeekRange()` called at render — unmemoized** — fixed in commit `528844fc`.
- [x] SCAN-999. **CampaignsPage used `as any` to access server data** — fixed in commit `244183bc`.
- [x] SCAN-992. **Catalog `modelResults` typed as `any[]`** — partial fix in commit `6733039e`. Added `CatalogDeviceModel` interface; `modelResults` state and the search-results map are now typed with `Array.isArray` runtime narrow before cast. `jobs` / `items` left loose (SCAN-992b follow-up) — a strict interface there would need to mirror many optional server fields including `items_upserted`, `pages_done`, `compatible_devices`, `stock_status`, etc. and ripple through UI readers.
- [x] SCAN-1005. **[HIGH/XSS] Communications MMS media URLs rendered unsanitized** — fixed in commit `5b890acb`. Added `safeMediaUrl()` helper (relative `/…` or absolute http/https only); both MMS rendering branches now filter the JSON-parsed array through the helper before rendering `<a href>` / `<img src>`. Poisoned `javascript:` / `data:` entries are dropped.
- [x] SCAN-1006. **ReviewsPage reply + public-posted icon buttons used only `title`** — fixed in commit `d5a70f5c`. Added `type="button"` + `aria-label` on both; inner icons now `aria-hidden`.
- [x] SCAN-1012. **ReviewsPage query key used inline object → cache miss each render** — fixed in commit `d5a70f5c`. Destructured to primitives `['customer-reviews', page, ratingFilter, repliedFilter]`; also added `staleTime: 30_000`.
- [x] SCAN-1007. **ExpensesPage list query missing `staleTime`** — fixed in commit `123179a9`. Added `staleTime: 30_000` to the list query.
- [x] SCAN-1011. **ExpensesPage form action buttons missing `type="button"`** — fixed in commit `123179a9`. Added `type="button"` to both Cancel and Add/Update buttons.
- [x] SCAN-1008. **Communications sms-conversations + sms-messages queries missing `staleTime`** — fixed in commit `c3f8e746`. Added `staleTime: 14_000` (15s interval) + `staleTime: 9_000` (10s interval) so re-mounts don't refetch on top of the polling cycle.
- [x] SCAN-1013. **Communications markReadMutation had no onError** — fixed in commit `c3f8e746`. Added `onError` that logs via `console.error` so unread-count desync is visible in telemetry.
- [x] SCAN-1010 (CashRegister half). **CashRegisterPage `history: any[]` + `onError: any`** — fixed in commit `55e41a3e`. Added local `CashRegisterHistoryEntry` interface (id, type union, amount, optional reason/name fields); history now typed; `Array.isArray` runtime narrow. Both mutation onError callbacks typed as `unknown` with narrow cast. Added `staleTime: 25_000` alongside the 30s refetchInterval. Expenses half split out as SCAN-1010b.
- [x] SCAN-1019. **LoanersPage "Mark Returned" button missing `type="button"`** — fixed in commit `da9b56fd`. Added `type="button"` + `aria-hidden` on the inner icon.
- [x] SCAN-1022. **LoanersPage list query missing `staleTime`** — fixed in commit `da9b56fd`. Added `staleTime: 30_000`.
- [x] SCAN-1023. **PrintPage fired ticket query with `Number(undefined)`=NaN** — fixed in commit `da9b56fd`. Parse once into `numericId`; gate the query with `enabled: Number.isFinite(numericId)`.
- [x] SCAN-1017. **PhotoCapturePage upload `catch (e: any)` with no toast** — fixed in commit `fe0b670c`. `catch` now types `e: unknown` + narrow shape cast; on failure shows both the inline error banner and a `toast.error` so mobile users see the failure even when scrolled.
- [x] SCAN-1018. **SetupPage `(setupData as any)` triple-cast** — fixed in commit `fe0b670c`. Added local `SetupStatusPayload` interface; `useQuery` generic now carries the typed shape so `wizard_completed`, `setup_completed`, `store_name` read cleanly without `as any`.
- [x] SCAN-1015+1016. **StepImport polling silently swallowed errors + captured stale `source` closure** — fixed in commit `e4c46884`. Captured `source` into `const pollSource` before `setInterval` so the callback always hits the correct status endpoint. Added a `consecutiveFailures` counter — after 5 failures in a row the poller clears the interval and surfaces a "Lost connection" error (previously the UI would spin forever against a dead backend). Also upgraded the outer `err: any` to `unknown` with narrow cast.
- [x] SCAN-1021. **LandingPage enterprise CTA used `window.location.href = 'mailto:…'`** — fixed in commit `b207613d`. Replaced the conditional-assignment pattern with a real `<a href="mailto:...">` element for the Enterprise tier; signup tier stays a `<button type="button">`. Browser now enforces the mailto protocol and the anchor is keyboard/screen-reader friendly.
- [x] SCAN-1010b. **ExpensesPage `exp: any` loop variable** — fixed in commit `fb92fcb1`. Added local `ExpenseRow` interface; `expenses` array narrowed via `Array.isArray`; `handleEdit` typed accordingly; `formatCurrency(Number(exp.amount) || 0)` coerces the legacy string-amount rows safely.
- [x] SCAN-984 (detail half). **EstimateDetailPage Send/Approve/Convert race** — fixed in commit `448ef7aa`.
- [x] SCAN-1024+1035. **[HIGH/XSS] UpgradeModal redirected to unvalidated URL + never reset `loading` on block** — fixed in commit `94676d26`. Parse checkout URL through `new URL()`, accept only `http:`/`https:` (rejects `javascript:`/`data:`); on success also call `setLoading(false)` so the button recovers if navigation is blocked by a popup blocker / beforeunload handler.
- [x] SCAN-1025. **[HIGH/XSS] `getIFixitUrl` returned admin `customUrl` without protocol check** — fixed in commit `94676d26`. Guard with `/^https?:\/\//i.test(customUrl)`; falls back to the generated search URL if validation fails.
- [x] SCAN-1026+1030. **SignatureCanvas loaded `initialValue` into `img.src` without `data:image/` check + Clear button missing `type="button"`** — fixed in commit `94676d26`. Guard `initialValue.startsWith('data:image/')` before assigning; Clear button now `type="button"` with `aria-hidden` icon.
- [x] SCAN-1028. **BackButton missing `type="button"`** — fixed in commit `b4377f41`. Added `type="button"` + `aria-hidden` on the arrow icon.
- [x] SCAN-1029. **CopyButton used only `title`** — fixed in commit `b4377f41`. Added `aria-label` that flips to "Copied to clipboard" on copy; inner icons now `aria-hidden`.
- [x] SCAN-1034. **Breadcrumb used array index as React key** — fixed in commit `b4377f41`. Key now derived from `href + label + index` — stable when items rearrange but still unique across duplicated labels.
- [x] SCAN-1033. **DateRangePicker Apply button missing `type="button"`** — fixed in commit `fd9e4368`. Added `type="button"` so the picker doesn't submit a parent filter form on Apply.
- [x] SCAN-1032. **API client interceptor used `as any` to access error envelope fields** — fixed in commit `3773b534`. Cast once to a local `{ code?: unknown; request_id?: unknown }` narrow type; field reads then flow through `typeof === 'string'` guards without any further casts.
- [x] SCAN-1027. **PinModal + UpgradeModal missing `role="dialog"` + aria semantics** — fixed in commit `ddc9b84c`. Both inner containers now carry `role="dialog"`, `aria-modal="true"`, `aria-labelledby` pointing at the title `<h2>` (added `id="pin-modal-title"` / `id="upgrade-modal-title"`). Close buttons gained `type="button"` + descriptive `aria-label`; decorative icons `aria-hidden`.
- [x] SCAN-1031. **CommandPalette silently swallowed search API errors** — fixed in commit `7dd611de`. Added `searchError` state; catch now logs via `console.error` and flips the flag; the "No results" block renders "Search unavailable — service not responding" when errored, distinguishing backend downtime from an empty result set.
- [x] SCAN-1038. **creditNotes POST `/:id/void` TOCTOU** — fixed in commit `82bb8bee`.
- [x] SCAN-1044. **loaners POST `/:id/loan` TOCTOU on device status** — fixed in commit `c24c140c`.
- [x] SCAN-1041. **notifications PUT `/focus-policies` body had no byte cap** — fixed in commit `810064b3`. Serialized JSON now checked against a 64 KB cap (`Buffer.byteLength(json, 'utf8')`) before the upsert; oversized payloads get a clean 400.
- [x] SCAN-1042. **notifications POST `/send-receipt` accepted any string with `@`** — fixed in commit `810064b3`. Now gated by `length > 0 && length <= 254 && /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/` — oversized or malformed addresses are rejected before SMTP.
- [x] SCAN-1040. **campaigns `/review-request/trigger` dereferenced `req.user!.id` on service-token path** — fixed in commit `752d25f2`. `audit(...)` now calls `req.user?.id ?? 0` so INTERNAL_SERVICE_TOKEN-authenticated requests don't throw a null deref.
- [x] SCAN-1045. **rma POST `/` missing rate limit + unbounded `items[]` loop** — fixed in commit `752d25f2`. Added `consumeWindowRate('rma_create', userId, 30/min)` + `RMA_ITEMS_MAX = 200` cap (both `!Array.isArray(items)` and length gated) before the per-item INSERT loop.
- [x] SCAN-1053+1054. **[HIGH/XSS] dunningScheduler renderTemplate didn't escape HTML or strip SMS control chars** — fixed in commit `3fa5e27c`. `renderTemplate` gained a `escape: 'html' | 'sms' | 'none'` mode. Email `html` render now uses `escape: 'html'` (escapeHtml on every substituted var); SMS body render uses `escape: 'sms'` (stripSmsControlChars). Subject and plain-text paths stay raw. A customer with a name like `<img src=x onerror=...>` can no longer inject markup into dunning emails, and control-byte-laced names can't poison UCS-2 SMS segments.
- [x] SCAN-1058. **`enqueueRetry` wrote phone/message/error unbounded to `notification_retry_queue`** — fixed in commit `5ca240bd`. Added `RETRY_MESSAGE_MAX=1600`, `RETRY_PHONE_MAX=32`, `RETRY_ERROR_MAX=500` caps; values sliced + string-checked before the INSERT. A runaway template can no longer bloat the queue table over time.
- [x] SCAN-1046. **crm `/customers/:id/photo-mementos` exposed raw `file_path`** — fixed in commit `573679c2`. Added local `sanitizeUploadPath()` helper that strips everything up to (and including) `/uploads/`, falling back to basename. Server response now exposes only the relative tail under uploads so absolute/OS-specific paths no longer leak.
- [x] SCAN-1043. **loaners POST `/:id/loan` missing rate limit** — fixed in commit `573679c2`. Added `consumeWindowRate('loaner_write', userId, 60/min)` before the existence/FK lookups; technicians can no longer spam loan creations in a tight loop.
- [x] SCAN-1052. **AutomationsTab rule name input had no length cap** — fixed in commit `3d1f80b5`. Added `maxLength={255}` to the rule-name input.
- [x] SCAN-1059. **AutomationsTab `err: any` in create/update onError** — fixed in commit `3d1f80b5`. Both handlers now type `err: unknown` + narrow shape cast before reading `response.data.message`.
- [x] SCAN-1051 (client half). **AutomationsTab email body had no client-side size cap** — fixed in commit `3d1f80b5`. Added `maxLength={10000}` to the body textarea. SCAN-1051b logged for the server-side sanitize/escape pass.
- [x] SCAN-1056. **slaBreachCron `markFirstResponseBreached` SELECT-then-INSERT race** — fixed in commit `63fe0052`.
- [x] SCAN-1049. **[HIGH] Catalog scraper stored supplier `imageUrl` without protocol/SSRF guard** — fixed in commit `e6d3b5a9`. After the existing `//` and `/…` prefix-fixup, the URL is now parsed through `new URL()` and dropped if the protocol isn't `http(s):` or the hostname matches an RFC1918/loopback/link-local pattern. Prevents `javascript:` XSS and SSRF targets (e.g. AWS metadata) from being persisted.
- [x] SCAN-1057. **retentionSweeper interpolated `table`/`dateColumn`/`redactColumn` into SQL without allowlist** — fixed in commit `e6d3b5a9`. Added `assertSqlIdent(name, field)` helper that enforces `^[a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*$`; both `applyRule` and `applyPiiRule` now assert identifiers before building SQL. Defense-in-depth so a future maintainer sourcing rules from config can't accidentally open a SQLi vector.
- [x] SCAN-1036. **creditNotes: all 5 handlers missing `asyncHandler` wrapper** — fixed in commit `191ab8dc`.
- [x] SCAN-1039. **campaigns mass-dispatch endpoints missing rate limit** — fixed in commit `789d88dc`.
- [x] SCAN-1047. **deposits GET `/` used hard `LIMIT 500` with no pagination** — fixed in commit `a0c7211e`. Replaced with `parsePage`/`parsePageSize` (default 50, max per `pagination.ts`); query now runs a `COUNT(*) + LIMIT ? OFFSET ?` pair in parallel; response includes a `meta.pagination` envelope consistent with other list routes.
- [x] SCAN-1050. **`liveSearchSupplier` made unbounded outbound HTTP calls** — fixed in commit `709b0a55`.
- [x] SCAN-984b. **EstimateListPage row action race** — fixed in commit `519c457b`.
- [x] SCAN-1020. **LandingPage per-card inline `onMouseEnter`/`onMouseLeave` handlers** — fixed in commit `5d0da082`. Added `.feat-card` + `.feat-card:hover` rules to the existing `<style>` block and applied the class to every feature card; dropped the inline handlers. CSS drives the hover animation now — no per-card function allocation on each render. Added `anyMutationPending = sendMut.isPending || convertMut.isPending || deleteMut.isPending`. All three row buttons now gate on it so a Convert (which navigates away) can't fire mid-Send/Delete. Also added `type="button"`, `aria-label`, and `aria-hidden` on icons as a drive-by a11y fix. Added process-level per-source bucket (30 searches / 60 s) via a Map; bucket reset computed on each call so clock drift doesn't accumulate. Throws a 429-tagged Error when exceeded, so caller can surface a clean rate-limit response. Added shared `rateLimitCampaignDispatch(req)` helper (3 dispatches / 60 s / user) and invoked it in `POST /:id/run-now`, `POST /birthday/dispatch`, `POST /churn-warning/dispatch` just after the admin gate. Blocks accidental dispatch loops burning SMS credit. All five (`GET /`, `GET /:id`, `POST /`, `POST /:id/apply`, `POST /:id/void`) now wrapped via `asyncHandler(...)`, matching the pattern used across the rest of the route tree. Unhandled rejections now flow to the central errorHandler middleware instead of hanging the response or crashing the process. Also loosened `validateId(raw: unknown, ...)` so the typed `req.params.id` (string | string[]) narrows cleanly. New migration `143_sla_breach_log_unique.sql` adds `UNIQUE INDEX ux_sla_breach_log_ticket_type ON sla_breach_log (ticket_id, breach_type)`. Service collapsed to `INSERT OR IGNORE ...; if result.changes === 0 return` — fully atomic idempotency; two concurrent workers can no longer double-log the same breach. The existence/availability SELECT stays (for clean 404/400) but the device flip is now `UPDATE ... WHERE id=? AND status='available'`; `changes === 0` returns 409 and the `loaner_history` insert is skipped, so two concurrent loans can't create duplicate history rows for the same device. Replaced SELECT + unconditional UPDATE with a conditional `UPDATE ... WHERE id=? AND status='open'` gated by `result.changes === 0`. Pre-SELECT retained only for clean 404. Two concurrent void calls (or void+apply) can no longer both flip the row — one wins, the other gets a 400/409 with the right message. Added `anyMutationPending = sendMut.isPending || approveMut.isPending || convertMut.isPending`. All three action buttons now gate on it, so clicking Convert mid-Send (or vice versa) is ignored until the first mutation resolves. List-page sibling split to SCAN-984b. Typed `useQuery` generics to `{ data?: Campaign[] }` / `{ data?: Segment[] }`; queryFn narrows via explicit cast inside (server-wrapper shape). Call site drops the `as any` chain entirely. Wrapped in `useMemo(() => getWeekRange(), [])`; the weekly-hours query key stays stable across re-renders (midnight boundary crossing still picked up on page reload). Regex swept 10 buttons across the 3 pages. aria-label audit deferred as SCAN-997b. Added `type="button"` to both Cancel and Collect buttons so the modal can't accidentally submit a parent form. Added `staleTime: 4500` (stats, 5s interval) and `staleTime: 2500` (jobs, 3s interval) so re-mounts don't trigger a redundant fetch on top of the active `refetchInterval` cycle. View/Edit/Deactivate links and the quick +1 / -1 stock buttons now carry `aria-label={`<action> ${item.name}`}`; inner icons marked `aria-hidden` so screen readers read each row action by its item name. Added `staleTime: 30_000` to 10 total `useQuery` calls across InventoryListPage (4), EstimateListPage (2), PurchaseOrdersPage (3), SerialNumbersPage (1). Focus events + route revisits stop hammering the backend with redundant paginated fetches. Added both, plus a visible focus ring and `aria-hidden` on the decorative close icon. Introduced `safeHref()` helper that accepts relative paths (`/uploads/...`) and absolute http(s) URLs only; anything else falls through to the `—` placeholder. Also upgraded `rel="noreferrer"` to `rel="noopener noreferrer"`. Rewrote `handlePrintBarcode` to build the print DOM programmatically: `doc.title` for the title text (value, not HTML), `createElement('style')` + `.textContent` for the CSS block, `createElement('img')` with `.src` + `.alt` + `.onload` for the barcode. Server-supplied sku/upc/name can no longer break out of the title element. Also added `noopener,noreferrer` to `window.open`. Helper now uses `React.useId()` to generate a stable id and clones the child element to inject `id` + `htmlFor`, so every field pair is programmatically associated without requiring each call site to pass ids by hand. Respects call-sites that already set `id`. Split the body into a thin `DashboardPage` router that picks either `<TechDashboard>` or a new `<AdminOrManagerDashboard>` component based on role. The admin component owns all ~30 post-gate hooks, so the technician path never reaches them. Hook counts are now stable across role changes, eliminating the React crash path. `onBack` from `confirm_slug` now clears `token`, `typedSlug`, and the error message before dropping to `request`; the `confirm_phrase → confirm_slug` back path clears `typedPhrase` + error too. A second request thus starts with a clean slate instead of silently failing against a server-consumed token. Wrapped the `.map()` body in an IIFE that hoists the max once before iterating. Enhanced the shared `FormLabel` helper with an optional `htmlFor` prop; wired the new-customer section's four fields (first name, last name, phone, email) with matching `id` attributes. Follow-up SCAN-961 logged for the remaining ~18 device/service labels in the same file.

## Closed 2026-04-23 (wave-47/48/49 web orchestration — hooks + utils + api + stores + components)

Autonomous web-improvement loop. Each item below was implemented, typechecked, and committed atomically. Moved out of TODO.md so the backlog reflects only open work.

- [x] SCAN-713. **useWebSocket silently bailed on missing accessToken with no retry after login** — fixed in commit `900d184c`. authStore now emits `bizarre-crm:auth-ready` after every path that installs a fresh access token (completeLogin, switchUser, each success branch of checkAuth); useWebSocket listens and reconnects deterministically instead of racing localStorage writes.
- [x] SCAN-846. **Hardcoded `/auth/refresh` path duplicated across API client** — fixed in commit `adad2496`. Extracted `AUTH_REFRESH_PATH` + `AUTH_REFRESH_URL` constants at module top; refresh POST URL and request-interceptor `includes()` now reference the shared constant.
- [x] SCAN-931. **Settings fetched from server were cast to `Record<string,string>` with no validation** — fixed in commit `c5b846d4`. `useSettings` now narrows the payload through `coerceSettings()`: refuses non-object values, skips nested objects/arrays/null, coerces number/boolean primitives to strings.
- [x] SCAN-932. **POS keyboard-shortcut listener re-attached every render when callers passed inline handler objects** — fixed in commit `507bf80d`. Handlers pinned in a ref, updated in a separate effect; listener-binding effect depends only on `enabled`, so window listener attaches exactly once per mount.
- [x] SCAN-933. **Draft autosave wrote unbounded text to localStorage — quota-fill DoS** — fixed in commit `88cc9222`. `useDraft` enforces a 100 KB cap before persist and wraps `setItem` in try/catch so QuotaExceededError never breaks the editing session.
- [x] SCAN-934. **`useUndoableAction` swallowed unmount-path errors silently** — fixed in commit `f956e146`. Replaced empty `.catch(() => {})` with `console.error` so silent data-loss failures surface in browser console / error telemetry.
- [x] SCAN-935. **Exported `cn()` utility had no return type** — fixed in commit `13ae478b`. Added `: string` annotation to satisfy the project type-safety rule.
- [x] SCAN-936. **Currency formatter silently fell back to USD for unknown codes** — fixed in commit `2453734a`. Logs the unknown code via `console.error` before the fallback formatter so misconfigured tenant currency settings surface in error telemetry.
- [x] SCAN-937. **`useSettings` swallowed fetch errors — callers couldn't tell failed-load from empty-settings** — fixed in commit `c5b846d4` (together with SCAN-931). Destructures `isError` + `error` from `useQuery` and returns them on the hook's public interface.
- [x] SCAN-938. **Super-admin axios client had no response interceptor — expired tokens silently failed every call** — fixed in commit `2bac8c1f`. Response interceptor clears `superAdminToken` on 401/403, shows a "Session expired" toast, and dispatches a new `bizarre-crm:super-admin-logout` CustomEvent. `TenantsListPage` listens and flips its local authenticated state.
- [x] SCAN-939. **JWT `exp` used without numeric validation — a malformed token caused a refresh storm** — fixed in commit `2b9c0afd`. Added `typeof payload.exp === 'number' && Number.isFinite(...)` guard before the arithmetic; the existing catch handles the throw by clearing the bad token.
- [x] SCAN-943. **`window.open('_blank')` missing `noopener,noreferrer` — reverse-tabnabbing risk** — fixed in commit `8389ae27`. Added the window-features string to the payroll-CSV export in `CommissionPeriodLock` and both print fallbacks in `PrintPreviewModal`.
- [x] SCAN-945. **QuickSmsModal buttons missing `type="button"` — accidental parent-form submit risk** — fixed in commit `27a1c972` (batched with SCAN-946 + SCAN-947).
- [x] SCAN-946. **QuickSmsModal recipient input not programmatically linked to its label** — fixed in commit `27a1c972`. Added `id="quick-sms-recipient"` + `htmlFor`.
- [x] SCAN-947. **QuickSmsModal SMS-template data typed as `any[]`** — fixed in commit `27a1c972`. Introduced local `SmsTemplate` interface; dropped every `any` in the template flow; added `Array.isArray` runtime guard against non-array server payload; tightened `onError` to `unknown` with shape narrowing.
- [x] SCAN-949. **GettingStartedWidget `trackableCount` recomputed every render** — fixed in commit `cc9215e1`. Lifted into `useMemo` with empty deps (STEPS is a module-level constant).
- [x] SCAN-941. **Plan-fetch errors silently swallowed on planStore** — fixed in commit `04df2cdb`. Added `error: string | null` to `PlanState`; cleared at fetch start + on success; populated from caught value on failure (Error / string / fallback). auth-cleared listener also wipes it. Feature gates can now distinguish transient-failure from empty-plan and offer a retry affordance.
- [x] SCAN-944. **ImpersonationBanner exit was a clickable `<div role="button">` with no keyboard handler** — fixed in commit `e76900f2`. Replaced with a real `<button type="button">` (full-width) that gets native Enter/Space keyboard activation + a visible focus ring; added `aria-label` including the tenant slug; marked decorative icons `aria-hidden`.
- [x] SCAN-948. **DataTable clickable rows + sortable headers unreachable by keyboard** — fixed in commit `007d6fef`.
- [x] SCAN-950. **`onError: (e: any)` in several team + inventory mutations bypassed safe narrowing** — fixed in commit `097197c8`. CommissionPeriodLock (create + lock mutations), TicketHandoffModal, and QuickAddInput now type `e: unknown` and narrow via `e && typeof e === 'object' && 'response' in e` before reading the server message. Keeps behavior identical on the happy path.
- [x] SCAN-942. **POS checkout line-item types were `unknown[]`** — fixed in commit `158fa261`.
- [x] SCAN-940. **Server-supplied upgrade-feature string passed unvalidated into the plan store** — fixed in commit `886a87ce`.
- [x] SCAN-958. **LeadListPage leaked console.error in prod on convert/delete failure** — fixed in commit `a51e3f2f`. Dropped the redundant `console.error` calls from both mutation `onError` branches (a toast is already shown with the server message). Also tightened `onError: (err: any)` to `unknown` with a narrow shape cast.
- [x] SCAN-959. **POS product search input missing aria-label** — fixed in commit `a51e3f2f`. Added `aria-label="Search products"` to the keyword input.
- [x] SCAN-952. **Invoice stats chart didn't refetch on filter change** — fixed in commit `8cfee31d`. Added `{status, dateRange}` to the `invoice-stats` query key so the chart refetches alongside the main invoice list.
- [x] SCAN-953. **Invoice status + method pie data recomputed every render** — fixed in commit `8cfee31d`. Both `.map(...)` transforms now wrapped in `useMemo` with the underlying distribution arrays as deps.
- [x] SCAN-951. **TicketListPage `handleAddNote` had no error handler — silent failure on save** — fixed in commit `c283ded7`. Wrapped the `ticketApi.addNote` call in try/catch; on failure, extracts the server message (via narrow shape cast) and shows a `toast.error`.
- [x] SCAN-955. **POS customer search silently swallowed network errors** — fixed in commit `aade00a1`. catch now logs + shows `toast.error('Customer search failed...')` so cashiers don't misread the empty list as "no matches".
- [x] SCAN-956. **POS `recentCustomers` IIFE recomputed every render** — fixed in commit `aade00a1`. Wrapped in `useMemo` with `[recentTicketsData]` deps. planStore now exports `UpgradeFeatureKey` + `isUpgradeFeatureKey()` type guard backed by a Set of valid keys (PlanFeatures keys + `ticket_limit`). The API client's 403 handler validates the server-supplied `feature` string through the guard before calling `openUpgradeModal`; malformed or unknown values are logged and ignored. Introduced `PosProductLineItem` and `PosMiscLineItem` interfaces matching the server's `pos.routes.ts` expectations; `CheckoutWithTicketInput` now uses the new types for `product_items` / `misc_items`.

- [x] ~~AUDIT-WEB-008.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **Optimistic invoice void diverges on error** — `InvoiceDetailPage.tsx:112-120` writes optimistic void to cache; if request fails after unmount, stale optimistic state remains until manual refresh. Fix: snapshot previous cache pre-mutation + `setQueryData` restore on error regardless of mount state.

Fix: typed return on `settingsApi.getStatuses()`; drop fallback.
- [x] ~~AUDIT-WEB-014.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **Customer Create email field has no format validation** — `CustomerCreatePage.tsx:144` only validates first_name; email is not `type="email"` nor regex-validated. - [x] ~~AUDIT-WEB-015.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **POS unified search does not cancel in-flight fetches** — `LeftPanel.tsx:22-122` three concurrent API calls; unmount mid-flight triggers state-on-unmounted warning. Fix: `isCancelled` flag in useEffect cleanup; guard all setters.
- [x] ~~AUDIT-WEB-016.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **ExpensesPage deleteMut has no onError** — `pages/expenses/ExpensesPage.tsx:52-55`. 403/500 produces no toast. Fix: `onError: (e) => toast.error(e?.response?.data?.message || 'Failed to delete expense')`.
- [x] ~~AUDIT-WEB-017.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **isBareHostname() treats LAN IP as multi-tenant** — `App.tsx:162` checks only `localhost`/`127.0.0.1`; `192.168.x.x` falls through. Fix: add `/^[\d.]+$/.test(host)` IP check routing to single-tenant unconditionally.
- [x] ~~AUDIT-WEB-018.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **POS tax-toggle buttons no aria-label** — `LeftPanel.tsx:407-418, 490-500, 530-535` only title= tooltip. Fix: `aria-label="Toggle tax for [item name]"` + `aria-pressed={item.taxable}`.

- [x] ~~AUDIT-WEB-020.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **Ticket merge does not invalidate tickets list** — `TicketDetailPage.tsx:92-105` only invalidates `['ticket', id]` + `['ticket-history', id]`. Fix: add `queryClient.invalidateQueries({queryKey:['tickets']})`.
- [x] ~~AUDIT-WEB-021.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **New-customer sub-form allows double-submit** — `TicketCreatePage.tsx:250-263` Save Customer button not wired to `createCustomerMut.isPending`. Fix: `disabled={createCustomerMut.isPending}`.
- [x] ~~AUDIT-WEB-022.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **Overdue invoice count silently = 0 on null/non-ISO due_date** — `InvoiceListPage.tsx:112` `new Date(due_date) < new Date()` returns false on NaN. Fix: guard `inv.due_date ? new Date(...) < now : false` + ensure server returns ISO strings.
- [x] ~~AUDIT-WEB-023.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **POS store `showSuccess: any` — shape unknown across 3 consumers** — `pages/unified-pos/store.ts:53-54` with 8 optional-chain fallbacks in SuccessScreen. Fix: `CheckoutSuccessPayload` discriminated union for (checkout, create_ticket) modes.

- [x] ~~AUDIT-AND-001.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **FCM PendingIntent requestCode=0 breaks multi-notification taps** — `service/FcmService.kt:107` uses hardcoded 0 + `FLAG_UPDATE_CURRENT`; older notifications navigate to newest. Fix: unique requestCode per notification via `notificationId.get()` or `System.currentTimeMillis().toInt()`.
- [x] ~~AUDIT-AND-002.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — both LoginScreen TLS call sites now use `buildProbeTlsClient(targetHost)` companion helper: DEBUG+LAN (loopback/RFC1918) installs platform-delegate trust manager that only bypasses when platform itself rejects; release OR public host uses platform defaults (full CA chain + hostname verification); `registerShop()` always targets CLOUD_DOMAIN → always platform CA.
- [x] ~~AUDIT-AND-003.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **Dark mode preference stored but never applied** — `MainActivity.kt:122` calls `BizarreCrmTheme {}` without darkTheme arg; `Theme.kt` defaults `darkTheme=true`. - [x] ~~AUDIT-AND-004.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **Checkout total loses precision via Double→Float→Double nav arg** — `AppNavGraph.kt:594` uses `NavType.FloatType`; $99.99 round-trips to 99.9899... . Fix: change nav arg to `NavType.StringType`, format as fixed-point string, parse with `toBigDecimal()` at destination.
- [x] ~~AUDIT-AND-005.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **`showBackupCodes!!` NPE on recomposition race** — `LoginScreen.kt:492`. Fix: replace `!!` with `.orEmpty()` or `?: emptyList()`.
- [x] ~~AUDIT-AND-006.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **Photo upload reads entire image into heap — OOM risk** — `PhotoCaptureScreen.kt:115-120` `copyTo(ByteArrayOutputStream)` no size cap. Fix: `ContentResolver.openFileDescriptor` + stat.size pre-check; cap at 20MB; downsample via `BitmapFactory.Options.inSampleSize` if over.
- [x] ~~AUDIT-AND-007.~~ FIXED 2026-04-19 — see commit. **Dashboard LazyColumn missing key=** — `DashboardScreen.kt:493, 522` `items(state.myQueue)` + `items(state.needsAttention)` no key lambda; positional diffing loses scroll/expansion state. Fix: `items(list, key = { it.id })`.

# Completed Tasks

## 2026-04-19

- [x] SEC-H103. **`JWT_SECRET` split into 5 scope-dedicated env vars + HKDF-SHA256 fallback derivation + production-fatal gates on CONFIG/BACKUP keys + transition-period verify fallback.** New env vars with per-scope HKDF `info`: `ACCESS_JWT_SECRET` (access tokens, 1h), `REFRESH_JWT_SECRET` (refresh tokens, 30d/90d), `CONFIG_ENCRYPTION_KEY` (AES-256-GCM for encrypted `store_config` values), `BACKUP_ENCRYPTION_KEY` (AES for `.db.enc` backups), `DB_ENCRYPTION_KEY` (reserved for SQLCipher — not wired yet). When any new-env is missing: derived via `hkdf(JWT_SECRET, salt='bizarre-crm-v1', info=<scope>)` with info = `access` / `refresh` / `config-enc` / `backup-enc` / `db-enc`. HKDF salt stays fixed domain-wide; info strings guarantee per-key independence (RFC 5869 correct pattern — salt alone doesn't need per-key uniqueness when info differs). Production-fatal gates in `packages/server/src/config.ts`: `configEncryptionKey` block fires `console.error` + `process.exit(1)` when `CONFIG_ENCRYPTION_KEY` unset/too short + `NODE_ENV=production`; `backupEncryptionKey` block identical for `BACKUP_ENCRYPTION_KEY`. No secret values logged — only var name + `randomBytes` generation command. Belt-and-suspenders also in `packages/server/src/utils/startupValidation.ts`. Transition-period verify fallback in `packages/server/src/utils/jwtSecrets.ts` `verifyJwtWithRotation()` — ordered try chain: (1) `config.accessJwtSecret` (current, dedicated or HKDF-derived), (2) `config.jwtSecretPrevious` (SA1-1 explicit rotation window), (3) `config.jwtSecret` (raw `JWT_SECRET` — transition fallback for tokens signed before this deployment). Only signature failures advance; expired/not-before errors propagate immediately. Once max 30-day refresh TTL expires, transition fallback can be removed. Callers migrated — access signing: `routes/auth.routes.ts:347 issueTokens`, `:1227 refresh rotation`, `:1417 pin-switch`, `routes/signup.routes.ts:362`. Refresh signing: `routes/auth.routes.ts:352`, `:1245`, `:1422`, `routes/signup.routes.ts:367`. Verify: `utils/jwtSecrets.ts:72`. Config encryption: `utils/configEncryption.ts:26 ENCRYPTION_KEYS[1]`. Backup encryption: `services/backup.ts:96 sidecar HMAC IKM` + `:265 getPassphrase() v1+`. Super-admin JWT (`SUPER_ADMIN_JWT_SECRET`) independent — untouched. `.env.example` updated with 5 new vars. Agent used `security-review` skill: HKDF salt/info pattern correct, no secret-name logging on boot-fatal, transition fallback strictly advances only on signature error (never on expiry). Verified: `cd packages/server && npx tsc --noEmit` → exit 0. Files: `packages/server/src/config.ts` + `packages/server/src/utils/configEncryption.ts` + `packages/server/src/services/backup.ts` + `packages/server/src/utils/jwtSecrets.ts` + `packages/server/src/utils/startupValidation.ts` + `packages/server/src/routes/auth.routes.ts` + `packages/server/src/routes/signup.routes.ts` + `.env.example`. Spawned via parallel Sonnet sub-agent (~94.9K tok, 46 tool_uses, 337s). (CRYPTO-H01 / BH-S003 / BH-S008 / BH-S009 / P3-PII-02)

- [x] SEC-H25. **`requirePermission` sweep across 7 tenant mutating route files — 72 handler gates added on top of existing role checks (defence-in-depth).** Pre-fix: many POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE handlers either had no gate (admin-only via middleware chain inherited from router.use) or inline `if (req.user.role !== 'admin')` — permission matrix was advisory. Middleware `requirePermission` already existed at `packages/server/src/middleware/auth.ts:189` — fail-closed on unknown roles (empty `ROLE_PERMISSIONS` → 403), custom-role matrix is authoritative when assigned (SEC-H18), admin bypass only fires when no custom role is pinned. 17 new permission constants added to `packages/shared/src/constants/permissions.ts`: `TICKETS_BULK_UPDATE`, `CUSTOMERS_MERGE`, `CUSTOMERS_GDPR_ERASE`, `CUSTOMERS_ARCHIVE`, `CUSTOMERS_BULK_TAG`, `INVENTORY_BULK_ACTION`, `INVOICES_VOID`, `INVOICES_BULK_ACTION`, `INVOICES_CREDIT_NOTE`, `REFUNDS_CREATE`, `REFUNDS_APPROVE`, `GIFT_CARDS_ISSUE`, `GIFT_CARDS_RELOAD`, `GIFT_CARDS_REDEEM`, `DEPOSITS_CREATE`, `DEPOSITS_APPLY`, `DEPOSITS_DELETE`. Role matrix: admin=all; manager=all except `users.manage` + `settings.import_export` + `customers.gdpr_erase`; technician=tickets CRUD+status, customers create/edit, `customers.bulk_tag`, inventory view, invoices view, SMS (no delete, no financial writes); cashier=POS + tickets/customers/invoices view + `invoices.record_payment` + `deposits.create` + `gift_cards.redeem`. File-by-file: `tickets.routes.ts` (28 handlers gated — create/edit/bulk_update/change_status per handler), `invoices.routes.ts` (6 — create/edit/record_payment/void/bulk_action/credit_note), `customers.routes.ts` (15 — create/edit/delete/merge/gdpr_erase/bulk_tag/archive/import_export/bulk-sms + assets/relationships/notes), `inventory.routes.ts` (16 — create/edit/delete/adjust_stock/bulk_action across items/kits/suppliers/POs/stocktake/receive-scan), `refunds.routes.ts` (4 — create/approve + credits use), `giftCards.routes.ts` (3 — issue/redeem/reload), `deposits.routes.ts` (3 — create/apply/delete; DELETE replaced inline `requireAdminDeposits()` with `requirePermission('deposits.delete')` + kept inline as defence-in-depth). Where inline role checks already existed, `requirePermission(...)` was ADDED (not replaced) so both layers enforce. Fixed 4 post-wiring TSC regressions in `inventory.routes.ts` (`/kits/:id`, `/:id` PUT) + `invoices.routes.ts` (`/:id` PUT, `/:id/credit-note`) — middleware-array form narrowed `req.params` to `string | string[]`; added explicit `Request<{id: string}>` generic to re-narrow. Agent used `security-review` skill. Verified: `cd packages/server && npx tsc --noEmit` → exit 0 after main-chat applied Request generic fix. Files: `packages/shared/src/constants/permissions.ts` + 7 tenant route files. Spawned via parallel Sonnet sub-agent (~172K tok, 165 tool_uses, 901s) — big sweep. (AZ-027)

- [x] SIGNUP-AUTO-LOGIN-TOKENS. **`POST /api/v1/signup` + `GET /signup/verify/:token` return `{accessToken, user, tenant}` + set `refreshToken` + `csrf_token` cookies — new-shop clients skip the re-login round-trip.** Pre-fix: dev-mode POST returned `{success:true, ...}` with no tokens; prod `GET /verify/:token` (post-SEC-H94 restored) redirected without setting auth state — iOS/Android clients had to prompt the user to log in again on the newly-provisioned tenant subdomain. Post-fix: private helper `issueSignupTokens(tenantSlug, req, res)` added to `packages/server/src/routes/signup.routes.ts` — NOT exported, scoped to module (avoided shared util file over-engineering; explicit inline copy of `auth.routes.ts` `issueTokens` pattern with back-reference comments). - [x] PROD105. **SMS sender ID + email from-address per-tenant via `store_config` — no longer forced to process-level env vars.** Pre-fix: `config.smsFrom` / `config.fromEmail` were single process-level values, so every tenant sent from the same sender — blocks compliance (brand identity, unsubscribe link, spam reputation). Post-fix adds two `store_config` keys to `ALLOWED_CONFIG_KEYS`: `sms_sender_id` (line 171) and `from_email` (line 184 + EMAIL_SETTINGS line 339 in `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts`). Validation regexes defined at module scope in both `packages/server/src/providers/sms/index.ts:49-50` and `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts:311-319`: `SMS_ALPHA_SENDER_RE = /^[A-Za-z0-9]{1,11}$/` (GSMA / 3GPP TS 23.040 §9.1.2.5 alphanumeric sender ID, 11 chars max), `E164_SENDER_RE = /^\+[1-9]\d{7,14}$/` (ITU-T E.164 §5.5.2, 8-15 digits), `EMAIL_FROM_RE = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/`. All three whitelist character classes — no whitespace/control chars pass, preventing SMPP/HTTP/SMTP CRLF header injection by construction. `sms_sender_id` accepts either alphanumeric OR E.164; `validateConfigValue` rejects anything matching neither. Send sites: `providers/sms/index.ts` `sendSmsTenant` — when caller didn't pass explicit `from`, resolves `store_config.sms_sender_id`, re-validates against both patterns at send-time (defense-in-depth against values stored before validator existed), passes `resolvedFrom` to `provider.send`; caller-supplied `from` (e.g. `sms_messages.from_number`) still takes precedence. `services/email.ts` `getSmtpConfig` — three-tier resolution `from_email → smtp_from → smtp_user`, validates `from_email` at read-time too; replaced `console.log/warn/error` calls in `sendEmail` with structured `emailLogger`. Fallback behavior: empty → next tier; invalid → warn log + next tier. System never hard-fails — always degrades to next valid sender with `info` log of source used. Neither key added to `ENCRYPTED_CONFIG_KEYS` or `SENSITIVE_CONFIG_KEYS` (non-credential identity fields). Key-injection prevented by `ALLOWED_CONFIG_KEYS` Set whitelist + `if (!ALLOWED_CONFIG_KEYS.has(key)) continue` guard in PUT /config. No domain-allowlist on `from_email` at code level — each tenant may own any domain; provider verification is operator-infra concern. Agent used `security-review` skill: SMTP header injection blocked by `\s` exclusion, SMS injection blocked by pure whitelist char classes, phishing mitigated by `adminOnly` gate on settings. Verified: `cd packages/server && npx tsc --noEmit` → exit 0 (after sibling agents merged). Files: `packages/server/src/providers/sms/index.ts` + `packages/server/src/services/email.ts` + `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts`. Spawned via parallel Sonnet sub-agent (~86.6K tok, 50 tool_uses, 322s).

- [x] SEC-H76. **Backup disk-space check async — promisified `execFile` with 5s timeout + fail-safe -1 on error.** catalogScraper wallclock half (60min ceiling + per-query + per-page cooperative check + partial_failure status) shipped earlier. Remaining half: `packages/server/src/services/backup.ts` `getFreeDiskSpace(dir)` used `spawnSync` (Windows PowerShell `Get-PSDrive` + Linux `df -B1 --output=avail`) blocking the event loop for up to 5s. Post-fix: function signature changed to `async (dir: string): Promise<number>` using `const execFile = promisify(require('child_process').execFile)` with `{timeout: 5_000, maxBuffer: 1024 * 16}`. Both Windows and Linux branches now `await execFile(...)`. Path validation (`assertSafePath(dir)`) + drive-letter regex (`^[A-Za-z]$`) preserved — no new command-injection surface since all argv is hard-coded except the regex-validated drive letter, and `{shell: false}` is default for `execFile`. On any error (timeout, ENOENT, non-zero exit, parse failure) logs warn `getFreeDiskSpace: OS command failed, returning pessimistic -1` and returns `-1`. Caller treats `free >= 0 && free < neededBytes` as blocking condition — a `-1` skips the block so backup proceeds (correct behavior: aborting a backup because the disk-space probe itself failed is worse than proceeding). Call site in `runBackup` changed to `await getFreeDiskSpace(backupDir)` (already inside async). Grep post-edit: `spawnSync` remains only in `listDrives()` (out-of-scope utility with hard-coded argv). - [x] SEC-H62. **Differential atomic UPDATEs on every stock mutation path — prevents concurrent-request double-credit / double-spend / over-receive.** Pre-fix: `UPDATE <table> SET qty = <computed-from-stale-SELECT>` pattern in POS return, inventory receive, ticket device/part delete, ticket bulk delete, gift card reload — two concurrent requests could both read the same pre-value and both write their deltas, over-crediting stock or balance. Post-fix, all 7 hot paths use `qty = qty + delta` / CAS-first atomic DELETE / guarded `AND qty + delta <= cap` patterns with `changes === 0` → 409 Conflict: (1) `giftCards.routes.ts:372` reload — `UPDATE gift_cards SET current_balance = current_balance + ? WHERE id = ? AND is_deleted = 0`; blocks credit to a soft-deleted card mid-race. (2) `inventory.routes.ts:1341-1348` PO receive inside `adb.transaction()` — `UPDATE purchase_order_items SET quantity_received = quantity_received + ? WHERE id = ? AND quantity_received + ? <= quantity_ordered`; blocks over-receive beyond ordered qty. (3) `tickets.routes.ts:1851` single delete — `UPDATE tickets SET is_deleted = 1 WHERE id = ? AND is_deleted = 0` promoted to FIRST (atomic CAS claim) before stock restore; only winner restores stock. (4) `tickets.routes.ts:3301` bulk delete — same CAS-first pattern, `changes === 0` → `break` (bulk tolerates partial success). (5) `tickets.routes.ts:2717` device delete — snapshot parts, `DELETE FROM ticket_devices` first (atomic gate), `changes === 0` → 409, then restore stock from snapshot. (6) `tickets.routes.ts:2928` part delete — `DELETE FROM ticket_device_parts` promoted first, `changes === 0` → 409, stock credit only after successful claim. (7) `tickets.routes.ts:2871` quick-add — `UPDATE inventory_items SET in_stock = in_stock - ? WHERE id = ? AND in_stock >= ?`, on `changes === 0` revert the INSERT and throw 409. Explicitly excluded: (8) `pos.routes.ts:2088` POS return already differential — SEC-H62 comment confirms. (9) `inventory.routes.ts:1519` stocktake — authorized absolute override; last-write-wins is correct policy; explicit exception comment. (10) `inventory.routes.ts:1585` scan-receive already differential — comment confirms. Grep verification: the only remaining `UPDATE inventory_items SET in_stock = ?` in the 4 routes is the documented stocktake exception. Agent used `security-review` skill. Verified: `cd packages/server && npx tsc --noEmit` → exit 0. Files: `packages/server/src/routes/{giftCards,inventory,tickets,pos}.routes.ts`. Spawned via parallel Sonnet sub-agent (~84.2K tok, 68 tool_uses, 373s). (C3-001, 003, 004, 010, 011)

- [x] SEC-M26. **Import worker 100-row batches + event-loop yield + periodic `PRAGMA wal_checkpoint(PASSIVE)`.** Pre-fix: `packages/server/src/services/repairDeskImport.ts` loops over large result sets using synchronous `db.transaction(...)` calls with hard-coded `100` batch literals, no event-loop yield between batches and no WAL checkpoint — a 50K-row import could starve HTTP keep-alive + WebSocket heartbeats for minutes and let the WAL file grow unbounded before the next auto-checkpoint. Post-fix: (a) two module-level consts `IMPORT_BATCH_SIZE = 100`, `IMPORT_CHECKPOINT_EVERY_N_BATCHES = 10`; (b) new async helper `yieldAndMaybeCheckpoint(db, batch)` — always `await new Promise(setImmediate)` so the event loop runs between batches; every 10th batch fires `db.pragma('wal_checkpoint(PASSIVE)')` (PASSIVE never blocks readers, safe to call opportunistically); (c) wired into all 5 importers: `importCustomers` / `importTickets` / `importInvoices` / `importInventory` / `importSms` — each loop now maintains its own `*BatchIndex` counter and calls `await yieldAndMaybeCheckpoint(db, batchIndex++)` immediately after each `db.transaction()()` close, before the progress-update callback. Hard-coded `100` literals in slice expressions swapped to `IMPORT_BATCH_SIZE` for consistency — runtime identical. Atomicity preserved — each batch is still its own transaction. Agent used `security-review` skill; verdict: no new SQL injection surface (`wal_checkpoint(PASSIVE)` is a string literal), no secrets introduced, no user-controlled data flows into the new code, parameterization + whitelist controls untouched. Verified: `cd packages/server && npx tsc --noEmit` → exit 0. Files: `packages/server/src/services/repairDeskImport.ts` only. Spawned via parallel Sonnet sub-agent (~73.7K tok, 47 tool_uses, 239s). - [x] SEC-M48. **Piscina worker pool hardened: `maxQueue 2000 → 200`, per-task 30s timeout via AbortController, queue-full → 503 + Retry-After.** Pre-fix: `packages/server/src/db/worker-pool.ts` `new Piscina({..., maxQueue: 2000})` + no per-task timeout. A single stuck query could pin a worker thread indefinitely, queue fills behind it, and the Piscina raw "queue is full" error leaked to the HTTP caller as a generic 500. Post-fix: (a) `TASK_TIMEOUT_MS = 30_000` const at module top; (b) new exported `WorkerPoolQueueFullError` class for clean `instanceof` downstream; (c) new `runWithTimeout(task)` private wrapper — arms AbortController with 30s timer, passes `{signal}` to `pool.run()`, clears timer on resolve, translates Piscina's `"queue is full"` message to `WorkerPoolQueueFullError`; all other errors re-thrown as-is; (d) all four exported runners (`dbGet`, `dbAll`, `dbRun`, `dbTransaction`) now use `runWithTimeout` instead of `getPool().run()`; (e) `middleware/errorHandler.ts` catches `WorkerPoolQueueFullError` (before generic AppError branch) and returns `503 { success:false, message:'Server busy, retry' }` + `Retry-After: 2` header. RFC-7231 compliant proxies (nginx / Cloudflare) honor the backoff. (f) `maxQueue: 200` is a hard backpressure cap — 10× lower than before; the 30s per-task timeout + 200-slot queue means worst-case serialized drain time is ~6000s if everything queues maximally, but in practice the abort signal frees threads much faster. (g) Pre-warm `SELECT 1` stays on `pool!.run()` (no runWithTimeout) — runs at startup before traffic, doesn't need AbortController. Agent used `security-review` skill — no info disclosure (error class name stays server-side), backoff header present, abort promptly frees thread. Verified: `cd packages/server && npx tsc --noEmit` → exit 0. Files: `packages/server/src/db/worker-pool.ts` + `packages/server/src/middleware/errorHandler.ts`. Spawned via parallel Sonnet sub-agent (~39.4K tok, 18 tool_uses, 122s). (REL-022)

- [x] SEC-H107. **Minimal CI workflow: build / audit / supply-chain jobs on PR + push:main.** Created `.github/workflows/ci.yml` (also whitelisted `!.github/**/*.yml` in `.gitignore` to override the blanket `*.yml` ignore earlier in the file). Three parallel jobs all pinned to Node 22.11 + `actions/checkout@v4` + `actions/setup-node@v4`: (a) **build** — `npm ci --ignore-scripts` (SEC-H111 aligned), `cd packages/web && npm run build`, `cd packages/server && npx tsc --noEmit`, `cd packages/management && npx tsc --noEmit`; (b) **audit** — `npm audit --audit-level=high` at root + each package.json; fails PR on high/critical; (c) **supply-chain** — `npm ls --all > /dev/null` at root + each package; fails on phantom deps / unresolvable tree. `permissions: contents: read` on the workflow — minimal GITHUB_TOKEN scope. `--ignore-scripts` consistent with SEC-H111 stance so CI installs never run lifecycle hooks. - [x] SEC-H108. **`app-builder-bin` moved from `dependencies` to `devDependencies` + pinned exact version (no `^` range).** `packages/management/package.json`: was `"dependencies": { ..., "app-builder-bin": "^5.0.0-alpha.10" }`, now `"devDependencies": { ..., "app-builder-bin": "5.0.0-alpha.10" }` (exact pin, no caret). Rationale: `app-builder-bin` is a build-time binary downloader used by `electron-builder` — not needed at runtime of the shipped app. Moving to devDeps removes it from the production install set (where it would otherwise be fetched on a prod deploy even though unused). Exact pin blocks an alpha-channel silent version bump (a `^5.0.0-alpha.10` spec would silently pick up `5.0.0-alpha.99` which might be breaking). Hand-edited, no agent — one-line change. (supply-chain)

- [x] SEC-H89. **Double-submit CSRF token on `/auth/refresh` + CSP `'unsafe-inline'` removed from `/admin` + `/super-admin`.** Pre-fix: `/auth/refresh` accepted any httpOnly-cookie POST unconditionally — browser cross-origin forms fired the refresh-token cookie automatically → session-pinning + token-refresh without user intent. Admin + super-admin CSP carried `script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'` + `script-src-attr 'unsafe-inline'` — permits any injected inline `<script>`, defeats the first line of XSS containment. Post-fix: (a) **CSRF** — token `crypto.randomBytes(24).toString('base64url')` (192-bit) set as `csrf_token` cookie alongside `refreshToken` on every login success path (`issueTokens()`). Cookie: `httpOnly=false` (JS must read for header injection), `SameSite=Strict`, `Secure` in production, same TTL as refreshToken. Rotated on refresh. Cleared on logout. `/auth/refresh` handler now checks: if request carries cookie `refreshToken` AND no body `refreshToken` (browser path, not Android), require `X-CSRF-Token` header to `crypto.timingSafeEqual` against `csrf_token` cookie. Mismatch → 403 + `audit('csrf_mismatch')`. Mobile clients (body refresh-token) skip the check — they don't use cookies at all. (b) **Web client plumbing** — `packages/web/src/api/client.ts`: new `getCsrfTokenCookie()` reader + axios interceptor injects `X-CSRF-Token` on every POST to `/auth/refresh`. Covers both `performRefresh()` and direct `authStore.ts` refresh calls. (c) **CSP tightening** — `adminCsp` changed from `script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; script-src-attr 'unsafe-inline'` → `script-src 'self'; script-src-attr 'none'`. (d) **Inline-script extraction** — `admin/index.html` 354-line `<script>` block → `admin/js/admin.js`. `admin/super-admin.html` 366-line block → `admin/js/super-admin.js`. All `onclick=` attributes replaced with `data-action=` + delegated `addEventListener` in the JS files. super-admin's dynamic-render paths (innerHTML) use `data-action/-slug/-session-id` attributes with listeners attached in `renderDashboard()`/`renderLogin()`. New `app.use('/admin/js', express.static(...))` serves the files; `script-src 'self'` permits them. (e) CORS on `/admin/api` + `/super-admin/api` unchanged. Agent used `security-review` skill. Verified: `cd packages/server && npx tsc --noEmit` → exit 0; web tsc too. Files: `packages/server/src/index.ts`, `routes/auth.routes.ts`, `admin/index.html`, `admin/super-admin.html` + new `admin/js/admin.js` + `admin/js/super-admin.js`, `packages/web/src/api/client.ts`. Spawned via parallel Sonnet sub-agent (~88.3K tok, 47 tool_uses, 388s) + `security-review`. (PUB-007, 008, 023)

- [x] SEC-H95. **Auto-update now requires a signed git tag + user-confirm dialog before `git pull` spawns.** Pre-fix: `management:perform-update` at `packages/management/src/main/ipc/management-api.ts:575` resolved project root, captured HEAD for rollback, audit-logged the launch, and immediately spawned `cmd.exe /c update.bat`. No signature check on the latest tag, no user-confirm — a compromised remote OR a local attacker who could write to the git remote URL could push a malicious tag + trigger auto-update in the background. Post-fix: (a) new `verifyLatestSignedTag(root)` helper — `git fetch --tags --quiet` (30s timeout), `git describe --tags --abbrev=0 --match 'v*'` to find latest semver tag (falls back to `git tag --sort=-version:refname --list 'v*'` when HEAD is off-tag), then `git verify-tag <tag>` — exits 0 only for valid GPG signature on the annotated tag object; non-zero for unsigned/expired/revoked. Failure → `TAG_VERIFICATION_FAILED` return; spawn never happens. Escape hatch `UPDATE_SKIP_TAG_VERIFY=true` (loud warn) for GPG-onboarding window. (b) After tag verify, `dialog.showMessageBox` — `'Install update to v1.2.3? [Install / Cancel]'` with `defaultId=1 cancelId=1` so Enter defaults to Cancel. Any non-Install → `UPDATE_CANCELLED` return. Window handle from `BrowserWindow.getFocusedWindow() ?? getAllWindows()[0] ?? null` so headless works. (c) `electron-builder.yml` stubs added with env-var references (Option A: `WIN_CERT_SUBJECT`, Option B: `WIN_CERT_FILE` + `WIN_CERT_PASSWORD`) — commented-out, ready to enable in CI. Signed tag = annotated tag object with GPG signature (not commit-level signature) — aligns with the repo's existing `REQUIRE_VERSION_TAG` opt-in in `githubUpdater.ts`. Agent used `security-review` skill. Files: `packages/management/src/main/ipc/management-api.ts` + `packages/management/electron-builder.yml`. Spawned via parallel Sonnet sub-agent (~52.3K tok, 31 tool_uses, 168s). (electron-002, 004)

- [x] SEC-H97. **Zod schemas + senderFrame-URL check + UNC/traversal-reject on every `ipcMain.handle` in `management-api.ts`.** Pre-fix: 48 IPC handlers accepted arbitrary `event.sender` messages without validating (a) origin, (b) payload shape, (c) path safety on disk-access handlers. A compromised renderer (XSS in an embedded view, malicious postMessage) could call any handler with any shape. Post-fix: (a) `assertRendererOrigin(event)` inspects `event.senderFrame?.url`; throws `IPC_ORIGIN_REJECTED` unless it's a `file://` URL pointing at the app; wrapped handler catches → structured `{success:false, message, offline:true}` reply. All 48 handlers now call it first. (b) 13 Zod schemas declared at module top; 14 handlers that accept meaningful args (login, 2fa-verify/setup, set-password, setup, stats-history, tenant CRUD/suspend/activate/repair, revoke-session, reenable-route, delete-backup, audit-update-result, browse-drive, create-folder) parse args before any side effect. (c) `assertSafePath` hardens `admin:browse-drive` + `admin:create-folder`: rejects raw UNC (`\\` or `//` prefix), rejects `..` pre-normalisation, `path.normalize` + `path.resolve`, rejects resolved `\\\\` prefix, rejects remaining `..`, drive-root allowlist (`[A-Za-z]:\` on Win / `/` on Unix). - [x] SEC-H98. **Cert fingerprint pinning on the Electron management api-client TLS connection.** Pre-fix: `packages/management/src/main/services/api-client.ts` connected to `https://localhost:443` with `rejectUnauthorized: false` (self-signed cert compat). A malicious process binding port 443 before the real server (port-squat at boot / sidecar-malware) could MITM the management session and harvest super-admin credentials + JWTs. Post-fix: (a) `resolveCertPath()` walks 5 levels up from `__dirname` to find `packages/server/certs/server.cert`; (b) `computePemFingerprint()` strips PEM headers, base64-decodes to DER, then `crypto.createHash('sha256').update(der).digest('hex')` — produces colon-separated uppercase-hex format matching Node's `cert.fingerprint256`; stored in module-level `EXPECTED_FINGERPRINT: string | null` (null = cert file absent at startup, pinning degrades with warn log). (c) `checkCertFingerprint(_hostname, cert)` — if pinning is armed, pulls `cert.fingerprint256`, `timingSafeStringEqual` against `EXPECTED_FINGERPRINT`, returns `Error('Cert fingerprint mismatch — possible port-squat / MITM\n  expected:...\n  presented:...')` on mismatch (error goes only to Electron main-process logs, never to a HTTP response). (d) `checkServerIdentity: checkCertFingerprint` injected on `httpsAgent.options` ONLY when the destination is loopback (preserves normal chain validation for any non-loopback target). (e) Startup-time INFO log of the expected fingerprint for ops triage. (f) No hardcoded fingerprint string — cert rotation auto-picks up on next Electron launch. Agent used `security-review` skill — confirmed timing-safe compare, no secrets in source, no fingerprint in user-facing HTTP, null-degradation is graceful. Verified: management tsc exit 0. Files: `packages/management/src/main/services/api-client.ts` only. Spawned via parallel Sonnet sub-agent (~40.7K tok, 36 tool_uses, 173s) + `security-review`. (electron-009)

- [x] SEC-H100. **Android release signing now fails closed when release-keystore properties file is missing.** Pre-fix: `packages/android/app/build.gradle.kts:65-95` `signingConfigs.create("release")` conditionally populated only when `~/.android-keystores/bizarrecrm-release.properties` existed; when absent, the `buildTypes.release.signingConfig = signingConfigs.getByName("debug")` fell back silently to the debug keystore. A CI misconfiguration or operator running `./gradlew assembleRelease` without the keystore would produce a debug-signed APK → Play Store rejection if caught; worst case a debug-signed release distributed (global debug key is well-known, opens the door to lateral updates). Post-fix: (a) `isReleaseBuild = gradle.startParameter.taskNames.any { it.contains(":assembleRelease", ignoreCase=true) || it.contains(":bundleRelease", ignoreCase=true) || it.equals("assembleRelease", ignoreCase=true) || it.equals("bundleRelease", ignoreCase=true) }` — gates the fail-closed check to only release tasks so `./gradlew assembleDebug` still works without the release keystore. (b) If `isReleaseBuild && !releaseKeystorePropsFile.exists()` → `throw GradleException("Release signing requires ~/.android-keystores/bizarrecrm-release.properties — build aborted. Expected path: <absolute>. Create the file with storeFile/storePassword/keyAlias/keyPassword properties.")` — build aborts before any unsigned or debug-signed artifact can be produced. (c) The defense is layered: even if `isReleaseBuild` misses an unknown task variant name, the `signingConfigs` + `buildTypes` block assignment is STILL guarded by `releaseKeystorePropsFile.exists()`, so no signing-bypass via creative task naming. Agent used `security-review` skill — confirmed no hardcoded secrets (keystore creds read from out-of-tree file), fail-closed is strict, debug path unaffected, no bypass vector. Files: `packages/android/app/build.gradle.kts` only (~+15/-5). Spawned via parallel Sonnet sub-agent (~21.8K tok, 4 tool_uses, 40s) + `security-review` skill. (BH-A010)

- [x] SEC-H101. **Android `fcmToken` migrated from plain SharedPreferences to `EncryptedSharedPreferences` (AES256-GCM + Android-Keystore-backed MasterKey).** Pre-fix: `packages/android/app/src/main/java/com/bizarreelectronics/crm/data/local/prefs/AppPreferences.kt` stored the FCM registration token in plain `prefs.getString("fcm_token")`. On a rooted device, a debug-flagged build, or ADB-accessible test device, another process holding the app's UID could read the token → attacker mints spoofed push notifications to the user's device. Post-fix: (a) added `encryptedPrefs: SharedPreferences = EncryptedSharedPreferences.create(context, "app_secure_prefs", MasterKey.Builder(context).setKeyScheme(MasterKey.KeyScheme.AES256_GCM).build(), PrefKeyEncryptionScheme.AES256_SIV, PrefValueEncryptionScheme.AES256_GCM)` — separate prefs file `app_secure_prefs` so the encrypted + plain stores coexist without migration-touching other fields. Matches the `DatabasePassphrase.kt` pattern already in the same package. (b) `fcmToken` getter/setter now reads/writes `encryptedPrefs` not `prefs`. Other AppPreferences fields unchanged (remain plain). (c) One-shot idempotent migration in `init`: if `prefs.getString("fcm_token")` is non-null, copy to encrypted + `remove("fcm_token")` from plain. Subsequent launches see nothing in plain prefs and the block is a no-op probe. (d) Gradle dep `androidx.security:security-crypto:1.1.0-alpha06` already present at `build.gradle.kts:186` — no new dep added. (e) File read-back confirms syntactic soundness (braces / getter-setter / init-block / imports). Agent used `security-review` skill — confirmed master key backed by Android Keystore, no log exposure of token, no hardcoded values. Files: `packages/android/app/src/main/java/com/bizarreelectronics/crm/data/local/prefs/AppPreferences.kt` only. - [x] SEC-H102. **`AuthInterceptor.clearAuthState()` now POSTs `/auth/logout` BEFORE wiping local prefs, so server-side session + refresh token are revoked on explicit logout.** Pre-fix: `packages/android/app/src/main/java/com/bizarreelectronics/crm/data/remote/interceptors/AuthInterceptor.kt:96-177` `clearAuthState()` just wiped `authPrefs` — server session row + refresh token survived locally-initiated logout until natural expiry (default 30 days). A cached refresh token on a previously-compromised device kept minting tokens after the user thought they'd logged out. Post-fix: (a) `clearAuthState(chain: Interceptor.Chain)` now takes the in-flight chain so it can derive the target server URL from `chain.request().url` (honors whatever `serverUrl` is configured; supports tenant subdomains). All 4 call sites (lines 80/110/148/159) already inside `intercept()` or `attemptTokenRefresh(chain)` pass `chain` cleanly. (b) Reads the current `accessToken` BEFORE the local wipe; builds a **bare** `OkHttpClient` inline (no Retrofit, no DI wiring) to avoid circular interception with AuthInterceptor itself — which was the whole reason the logout call couldn't just use `AuthApi.logout()` from DI. (c) Synchronous `.execute()` is safe: AuthInterceptor's `intercept()` runs on OkHttp's background thread. `callTimeout(LOGOUT_TIMEOUT_MS = 2_000L, MILLISECONDS)` bounds it so a wedged server can't delay UX past 2 seconds. (d) POST `/api/v1/auth/logout` with `Authorization: Bearer <accessToken>` + existing permissive `hostnameVerifier { _,_ -> true }` (matches the project's existing self-signed-cert policy). (e) On ANY exception: `Log.w(TAG, "Best-effort logout failed, proceeding with local wipe")` — never rethrown. `authPrefs.clear()` runs last, unconditionally. Agent used `security-review` skill — confirmed token carried only in Authorization header, errors log-only (no sensitive data in message), local wipe guaranteed after any result. Files: `packages/android/app/src/main/java/com/bizarreelectronics/crm/data/remote/interceptors/AuthInterceptor.kt` only. - [x] SEC-H78. **Single-query kanban + tv-display endpoints (N+1 → 1+1 and 51 → 1).** Pre-fix: kanban handler in `packages/server/src/routes/tickets.routes.ts:1130-1176` did `Promise.all(statuses.map(s => adb.all(SELECT ... WHERE status_id=?)))` — one round-trip per status column. TV-display at :1362-1389 additionally fired `Promise.all(tickets.map(t => adb.get(device_name WHERE ticket_id=?)))` — one round-trip per ticket row (up to 51 queries for a 50-row TV frame). Post-fix: (a) **Kanban** collapsed to a subquery `SELECT ... , ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY t.status_id ORDER BY t.updated_at DESC) AS rn FROM tickets t WHERE status_id IN (?,?,?,...) AND <filters>` outer-filtered by `WHERE rn <= 500`. JS groups the flat result into `Map<statusId, rows[]>` and the existing `statuses.map(...)` rebuild reconstructs the `{ status, tickets[] }` response shape byte-identical to before. Query count N+1 → 2. (b) **TV-display** uses `LEFT JOIN ticket_devices td ON td.ticket_id = t.id` + `GROUP_CONCAT(td.device_name, '||')` + `GROUP BY t.id`. JS splits on `'||'` to restore `device_names: string[]`. Query count 51 → 1. (c) Response shapes preserved byte-for-byte; filters (assignee / search / date range) all still apply.
