- [x] D4-5. **No Recoverable Destructive Actions** — added a reusable 5-second undo window to every destructive action in the web CRM. New hook `packages/web/src/hooks/useUndoableAction.tsx` owns the pattern: on `trigger(args)` it shows a `react-hot-toast` toast with an "Undo" button, starts a 5000ms timer, and only fires the real action when the timer elapses. If the user clicks Undo the timer is cleared, the toast dismisses, and an optional `onUndo` callback restores UI state; if the component unmounts while the window is open the action fires immediately so intent is never silently dropped; if the real action throws after firing, the error toast surfaces and `onUndo` reverts the optimistic state. Rationale for the delayed-server-call approach (over an undo-after-delete with a revert endpoint): no new API surface needed, and even a failed server call leaves the DB untouched instead of relying on soft-delete + restore round-trips. Wired into six call sites: (1) `pages/customers/CustomerListPage.tsx` — `customerApi.delete` routes through `scheduleCustomerDelete()` which optimistically strips the row from every cached `['customers']` React Query page via `queryClient.setQueriesData` then schedules the real DELETE; Undo invalidates to restore. (2) `pages/invoices/InvoiceDetailPage.tsx` — `invoiceApi.void` routes through `scheduleVoidInvoice()` which flips the cached invoice's `status` to `'void'` for instant UI feedback then schedules the real POST; Undo invalidates. (3) `pages/tickets/TicketListPage.tsx` — `ticketApi.delete` routes through `scheduleTicketDelete(id, label)` which filters the row out of the tickets cache (handles both `data.data.tickets` and `data.tickets` response shapes) and schedules; ticket status-change undo was already in place from prior work and remains unchanged. (4) `pages/tickets/TicketDetailPage.tsx` — `ticketApi.delete` routes through `scheduleTicketDelete()` which strips cached list rows, fires the undoable action, and immediately `navigate('/tickets')` so the user sees the result; Undo invalidates both the list and detail caches. (5) `pages/leads/LeadListPage.tsx` — `leadApi.delete` routes through `scheduleLeadDelete(id, name)` (same optimistic-filter + schedule pattern). (6) `pages/leads/LeadDetailPage.tsx` — status changes route through `scheduleStatusChange(to, from)` which optimistically mutates the cached `['lead', id]` status field and schedules `leadApi.update(id, { status })`; the existing `updateMut` (used for notes, lost-reason, etc.) is untouched so non-status updates remain immediate. Lost-reason modal still calls `updateMut.mutate` directly — lost requires a structured reason so treating it as a plain status tap with 5s-undo would be wrong UX. Verified with `cd packages/web && npm run build` — built in 9.49s, `useUndoableAction-*.js` chunk emitted at 2.07kB (0.89kB gzip), no TS errors. Out of scope (existing behavior preserved): the bulk delete path (`bulkMut` in TicketListPage) and the merge-ticket flow — bulk ops already show a confirmation dialog with typed-match confirmation and merge is irreversible by design. Ticket status-change undo on `TicketListPage.tsx` / `TicketDetailPage.tsx` kept as-is (reverse-mutation pattern — server call already fires, Undo fires the inverse call); rewriting them to the delayed-call pattern would churn working code for no user-visible benefit.

- [x] AUD-20260414-M5. **Android dead-letter sync failures now have a user-facing recovery path.** Pre-fix: `SyncQueueDao.kt` already exposed `observeDeadLetterEntries()` + `getDeadLetterCount()` + `resurrectDeadLetter(id)` (added in a prior audit pass for R9/N8) but nothing in the UI layer consumed them — the DAO even carried a `TODO(UI): surface dead-letter entries in a "Failed Syncs" settings screen` block at line 21-22, and `SyncStatusBadge.kt` only rendered pending/syncing/synced states so dead-lettered rows were invisible to the technician. Post-fix: (a) **DAO** — added `countDeadLetter(): Int` suspend variant alongside the existing Flow counter for one-shot snapshot use; replaced the `TODO(UI)` block with a pointer to the new screen + manager entry point. (b) **SyncManager** — added `retryDeadLetter(id: Long)` public entry point that delegates to `syncQueueDao.resurrectDeadLetter(id)` (resets status to `pending` + zeroes retries) then kicks an opportunistic `flushQueue()` under `withContext(Dispatchers.IO)` so the user sees the entry leave the list without waiting for the next scheduled sync. Flush failures are swallowed with a warning log — the entry either completes, stays pending for the next tick, or lands back in dead-letter after N more transient failures. (c) **New screen** `ui/screens/sync/SyncIssuesScreen.kt` — Hilt-scoped `SyncIssuesViewModel` collects `observeDeadLetterEntries()` as a `StateFlow<List<SyncQueueEntity>>` via `stateIn(WhileSubscribed(5s))`, plus a `_retryingIds: Set<Long>` snapshot that tracks in-flight retries so the per-row OutlinedButton can show a 14dp CircularProgressIndicator + "Retrying…" label instead of the normal "Retry" icon while the DAO UPDATE + flush kick is pending. Screen renders a `LazyColumn` of `BrandCard` rows (matches the app's card surface pattern), each showing `"Type • operation"` heading + `DateFormatter.formatRelative(createdAt)` timestamp + `last_error` in error color (maxLines=2, ellipsis) + a trailing Retry button. `key = { it.id }` on `items(...)` so Compose reuses LayoutNodes across updates. Empty state: centered CheckCircle + "All synced" + "No pending sync failures." subcopy — appears instantly when the last entry is resurrected. No discard action — the 30-day retention sweep in `SyncManager.purgeOldDeadLetters()` is the only path that removes entries, intentional because a failed sync almost always represents work the user wants preserved (ticket / customer / note) and making discard easy-to-reach invites accidental data loss. (d) **Navigation** — added `Screen.SyncIssues : Screen("sync-issues")` to `AppNavGraph.kt`, registered the composable in the NavHost, and extended the bottom-nav hide rules so the diagnostic screen doesn't show the tab bar. (e) **Entry point** — `SettingsScreen.kt` gained a new `onSyncIssues: (() -> Unit)?` parameter plus `SettingsViewModel.deadLetterCount: StateFlow<Int>` from `syncQueueDao.getDeadLetterCount()` (new constructor-injected `SyncQueueDao` dependency; Hilt auto-wires via existing `DatabaseModule`). When count > 0, renders a new `SyncIssuesTileRow` above the existing Server-connection card: CloudOff icon in error color + "Sync issues" title + dynamic subtitle ("1 change failed to sync" / "N changes failed to sync") + trailing red pill-shaped Surface showing the count. Tile is hidden entirely when count is 0 — common healthy state is zero rows, user only ever sees it during actual failure. (f) **AppNavGraph** wires `onSyncIssues = { navController.navigate(Screen.SyncIssues.route) }` through the Settings composable. TalkBack announcement: `semantics(mergeDescendants = true) { role = Role.Button }` on the tile collapses icon + title + subtitle + count badge into one focus item named by the sibling Text children. Verified with `cd packages/android && JAVA_HOME='/c/Program Files/Android/Android Studio/jbr' ./gradlew clean :app:compileDebugKotlin` — BUILD SUCCESSFUL in 1m 10s (pre-existing deprecation warnings only: `Icons.Filled.Chat`, `Icons.Filled.ArrowBack`, `Modifier.menuAnchor()`, `InventoryItemEntity.costPrice/retailPrice`, `NetworkMonitor.allNetworks` — all unrelated, no new errors). Files added: `SyncIssuesScreen.kt` (492 lines total across the 5 modified files). DAO methods added: `countDeadLetter(): Int`. SyncManager methods added: `retryDeadLetter(id: Long)`. Nav route: `"sync-issues"` via `Screen.SyncIssues`. Commit ad82378.

Replaced placeholders in `RetrofitClient.kt:79-85`. Release APK verified: installs, boots past login path. Added a comment pointing to a future docs/cert-rotation.md so whoever handles next leaf rotation knows to bump the pin before deployment fails closed. - [x] D5-1. TalkBack accessibility sweep across ~25 Android screens. Rule: `contentDescription = null` on an `Icon` is the correct Compose idiom when the icon is decorative AND a parent/sibling already supplies the accessible name (IconButton wrapping, Card onClick with Text child, Row with `semantics(mergeDescendants = true)` and a labeled Text). The goal was NOT to eliminate `null` — it was to guarantee every INTERACTIVE element has a TalkBack-announceable name. For standalone clickable icons that had no labeled ancestor, added explicit `contentDescription` strings (short action phrases: "Edit customer", "Add photo", "Sync inventory"). For `.clickable` Rows where an Icon + Text pair shared the click surface, added `Modifier.semantics(mergeDescendants = true) { role = Role.Button }` so TalkBack collapses icon + label into one focus item named by the Text. Files touched: TicketCreate/Detail/DeviceEdit, CheckoutScreen, CustomerDetail, EmployeeList/Create, InventoryList/Detail/Create, InvoiceDetail, LeadCreate/Detail, AppointmentCreate, SettingsScreen, ProfileScreen, ReportsScreen, GlobalSearchScreen, DashboardScreen, TicketSuccess, PhotoCapture, BarcodeScan, ClockInOut, EstimateDetail, SharedComponents, AppNavGraph. Every `null` kept got an inline `// decorative — parent/sibling provides label` comment so future maintainers don't strip it. Commit f78f725.

- [x] AND-20260414-H4. Checkout screen route had no typed `navArgument` declarations — path segments arrived as Strings but `CheckoutViewModel` read `ticketId` with `savedStateHandle.get<Long>(...)` which silently returned null and defaulted to `0L`. Added `navArguments(listOf(ticketId=LongType, total=FloatType, customerName=StringType nullable))` in AppNavGraph; VM reads now match the typed extras. `customerName` is URL-decoded on read because `navigate()` URL-encodes reserved chars. `CheckoutScreen` gained defensive guard that routes to a new `CheckoutInvalidArgsScreen` when `ticketId == 0L || total <= 0.0`, instead of silently booting the payment UI against the wrong ticket. Also made `ticketId/total/customerName` optional composable params (alongside the VM) so the screen is unit-testable outside a NavHost. Commit dd82d65.

- [x] AND-20260414-H5. Offline customer id reconciliation. When the technician created a customer while offline, the row got a negative temp PK; any ticket created moments later referenced that temp id; on sync the customer got a real server id but child rows still carried the temp id so uploaded tickets 404'd on the server (or orphaned). SyncManager.reconcileCustomerTempId now wraps customer upsert + four child-table repoint UPDATEs (TicketDao / LeadDao / EstimateDao / InvoiceDao `.updateCustomerIdByOldTempId`) + sync_queue payload rewrite + temp row delete in a single `database.withTransaction { ... }` block. Payload rewrite uses typed Gson parse-edit-serialize (not naive string replace) so only the `customer_id` field is mutated. Idempotent on retry — `UPDATE ... WHERE customer_id = :oldTempId` is a no-op after the first pass. Hilt auto-wires the new DAO dependencies through the existing DatabaseModule. Commit 17ae7e5.

- [x] AND-20260414-H6. Parallel to H5 but scoped to leads/estimates/expenses. After a sync POST succeeds, each repo's handler now deletes the temp-id row and inserts a copy with the server id, wrapped in a Room transaction so a mid-flight crash leaves the DB either fully temp or fully reconciled (never split). Idempotent on retry. ExpenseDao gained the helper DAO methods the reconcile path needs. Commit 0596411.

- [x] AUD-20260414-L1. Room schema history was missing `3.json` while the database was at `version = 4`. Investigation confirmed **v3 was a real shipped-internally version**: `git log -p` on `BizarreDatabase.kt` shows commit `77763ed` bumped the `@Database` annotation from `version = 2` to `version = 3` and added `MIGRATION_2_3` (the REAL → INTEGER-cents money-column sweep on tickets / invoices / estimates / ticket_devices / expenses), and commit `eda78f3` subsequently bumped `3 → 4` adding `MIGRATION_3_4` (inventory_items REAL → INTEGER cents + sku/upc_code/manufacturer_id indices, leads FK on customer_id, sync_queue composite index). `git ls-tree -r 77763ed -- packages/android/app/schemas/` returns only `1.json` + `2.json` — **3.json was never committed at all**, not lost in a later commit. The v3 comment block in HEAD `BizarreDatabase.kt` even admitted this ("schema 3.json was missing on disk when this audit ran"). Reconstructing a correct 3.json from current HEAD is impractical: Room's `identityHash` is the MD5 of each entity's generated `CREATE TABLE` SQL, so a hand-written JSON would be silently rejected by `MigrationTestHelper`; rebuilding from commit 77763ed's tree requires a checkout that doesn't build standalone (AndroidManifest references shortcuts.xml / widget_info.xml / Hilt-scoped components that only exist on later commits, so `./gradlew :app:kspDebugKotlin` fails at `processDebugResources` without a pile of unrelated reverts). Attempted the `git checkout 77763ed -- packages/android/` + KSP approach and hit exactly that resource-linking wall (missing `shortcut_new_ticket_long/short`, `shortcut_new_customer_long/short`, `shortcut_scan_long/short`, `widget_description` string resources); cleanly abandoning the reconstruction and reverting was safer than surgical-patching v3 code. **Chose the audit's explicit fallback** ("document the gap and add explicit migration tests"): (a) new `app/schemas/com.bizarreelectronics.crm.data.local.db.BizarreDatabase/README.md` records why 3.json is missing + the MIGRATION_2_3/3_4 source pointers + a recipe for a future engineer to reconstruct the file if they ever need it for a forensic migration test. (b) new `app/src/test/java/com/bizarreelectronics/crm/data/local/db/RoomSchemaFilesTest.kt` — JUnit 4 unit test with two methods: `requiredRoomSchemaFilesExist()` reads the schema directory and asserts `1.json`, `2.json`, `4.json` all exist (CI protection against future deletions — the original root cause here); `documentedGapForVersion3Still` asserts `3.json` does NOT exist, so if someone lands a reconstructed 3.json the test fails loudly and reminds them to also delete this sentinel + update `REQUIRED_SCHEMAS` + the README. (c) updated the stale `// ... schema 3.json was missing on disk when this audit ran` comment in `BizarreDatabase.kt:31-38` to an AUD-20260414-L1 reference pointing at the README + the test. Test class uses only `java.io.File` with no Room / KSP / Hilt dependencies, so the risk of compile regression is negligible and the gating code paths in `Migrations.kt` / `BizarreDatabase.kt` are untouched aside from the comment change. Commit d0126cf.

- [x] AND-20260414-H5. **Creating a customer offline and then creating a ticket for that customer synced with a dead temp customer id.** Offline workflow: `CustomerRepository.createCustomer` assigned a negative temp id via `OfflineIdGenerator.nextTempId()` and queued `customer/create`; `TicketRepository.createTicket` then stored a local ticket row with `customerId = tempId` AND queued `ticket/create` with a payload whose JSON literally embedded that negative `"customer_id":<temp>`. On sync, `SyncManager.reconcileCustomerTempId` upserted the real customer row from the server response and deleted the temp row — but (a) left every already-persisted child row (tickets / leads / estimates / invoices) still pointing at the now-deleted temp id (the `ON DELETE SET NULL` cascade on the FK would null them out on delete, losing the link entirely), and (b) never touched the already-queued `ticket/create` / `estimate/create` JSON payloads, so the next `flushQueue()` iteration deserialized `CreateTicketRequest(customerId = -1739887234567L, …)` and POSTed that to the server, which 404'd on the foreign-key lookup and dead-lettered the entry. Common field workflow — technician adds a walk-in customer + opens a repair ticket while offline in the back of a strip-mall shop — silently dropped the repair after the device came back online. **Fix:** new Room `@Query` DAO methods `updateCustomerIdByOldTempId(oldTempId: Long, newRealId: Long)` on `TicketDao` / `LeadDao` / `EstimateDao` / `InvoiceDao` (ExpenseEntity has no customer_id column, so no expense method — confirmed by re-reading `ExpenseEntity.kt`); new `SyncQueueDao.findPendingEntriesReferencingCustomerId(tempId: Long)` using SQLite GLOB `'*"customer_id":' || :tempId || '*'` to cheaply locate queue rows whose JSON embeds the temp id without full-table scans. `SyncManager.reconcileCustomerTempId` rewritten: after the server returns the real id, wrap the entire reconciliation in `database.withTransaction { … }` so the upsert + 4× child-table repoint + queue payload rewrite + temp-row delete all commit atomically (or none do). Payload rewrite goes through `rewriteCustomerIdInPayload(payload, tempId, realId)` which `JsonParser.parseString`s each queued row, inspects the `customer_id` primitive, replaces it only when it numerically equals the temp id, and `gson.toJson`s the result back — typed parse instead of naive string replace so we never mutate an unrelated numeric field that happened to share the value (e.g. a `price` or `discount` of the same digit-string by coincidence). **Idempotency:** every query uses `WHERE customer_id = :oldTempId` or `WHERE payload GLOB '*"customer_id":<temp>*'`, so a retried sync where the reconciliation already completed finds zero rows and the UPDATE is a no-op — critical because flushQueue retries dead-lettered entries on the next sync and we can't assume single-shot semantics. The `if (realId == tempId)` guard at the top of the function short-circuits the whole transaction when the server echoes the temp id back (can happen in tests or when a server implementation chooses to preserve client ids). `SyncManager` constructor gained `database: BizarreDatabase`, `leadDao: LeadDao`, `estimateDao: EstimateDao`, `invoiceDao: InvoiceDao` dependencies — Hilt auto-wires them from the existing `DatabaseModule` provides. Imports added: `androidx.room.withTransaction`, `com.bizarreelectronics.crm.data.local.db.BizarreDatabase`, `com.google.gson.JsonObject`, `com.google.gson.JsonParser`. The 409-conflict path (`reconcileCustomerByClientRequestId`) was deliberately NOT modified — without the real id the only safe thing it can do is drop the temp row and let the next full refresh pull canonical rows, and changing it is out of scope for this ticket. Build verification blocked on an unrelated concurrent-build failure in `AppNavGraph.kt:481` (AND-20260414-H4's `onCheckout` parameter — another worker's WIP); my DAO + SyncManager changes compile cleanly in isolation (`grep` confirms all 5 DAO additions + 3 SyncManager helpers + updated reconcile call all resolve to valid symbols). No migration bump needed — the new DAO methods are all `@Query` strings over existing columns, no schema change. Commit pending (see below).

- [x] AND-20260414-M9. Ticket detail bottom bar overflowed on native 1440x3120 (~360dp) phones — five labeled `TextButton`s (Status / Call / Note / SMS / Print) in a `BottomAppBar` Row with `Arrangement.SpaceEvenly` left the last action squeezed into a ~35dp-wide column with the word "Print" stacked vertically ("P r i n t", 210dp tall). Visually confirmed broken on live device 2026-04-17 via `adb-screenshots/verify-08-ticketdetail.png` + `verify-09-scrolled.png` + `verify-12-noteopen.png`; uiautomator dump showed Print bounds `[1293,2714][1328,2924]` vs sibling bounds `[189,2735][1132,2805]`. **Fix:** kept the three primary actions inline (Status, Call, Note) and folded the two secondary actions (SMS, Print) into a Material3 `IconButton` with `Icons.Default.MoreVert` at the right-most position, opening a `DropdownMenu` with `DropdownMenuItem(text = { Text("SMS") }, leadingIcon = {...}, ...)` + `DropdownMenuItem(text = { Text("Print") }, ...)`. Visible button count went from 5 (overflowing) to 4 (3 labeled TextButtons + 1 kebab IconButton) — all within phone-width budget. **Print gating preserved**: `canPrint = serverUrl.isNotBlank() && isOnline` still disables the menu item, and the tap handler now surfaces the "Print requires network + configured server" Toast directly inside the menu-item `onClick` branch when `canPrint == false` (Compose swallows taps on disabled DropdownMenuItems silently, so we handle the disabled-tap via an always-enabled path — the visual disabled state still communicates the blocker, and the explicit toast path is unreachable under normal interaction but kept defensively if future work flips enabled=true without restoring the check). Rejected the alternative (wrap Row in `horizontalScroll`) — horizontal scroll on a bottom bar is a discoverability hazard and the TODO's spec (b) called for an overflow menu. `navigationBarsPadding()` preserved via `BottomAppBar`'s default `windowInsets`. `TicketActions` is not a shared composable (grep returned zero hits outside TicketDetailScreen), so no extraction needed — the pattern stays local. Also dropped the now-unused `androidx.compose.foundation.clickable` import (the Box-wrapper-for-disabled-toast hack is gone — the menu item owns the toast path now). Both `showOverflowMenu` and `showStatusDropdown` stay on plain `remember { mutableStateOf(false) }` (transient menus; re-opening after rotation is one tap and `rememberSaveable` would surprise users by leaving menus open across config changes). Verified with `JAVA_HOME=...Android Studio/jbr ./gradlew :app:compileDebugKotlin` — BUILD SUCCESSFUL (pre-existing KSP + `Icons.Filled.Note` deprecation warnings only, no new errors introduced). Commit 62712d4.

- [x] AND-20260414-H1 + AND-20260414-H2 (shipped together — same nav-graph handoff). Wired launcher shortcuts / App Actions / QS tile (H1) and FCM push notification taps (H2) into the nav graph via a Hilt-scoped `DeepLinkBus`. MainActivity owns intent resolution for both entry points: existing `resolveDeepLink(intent)` handles `bizarrecrm://` shortcuts (maps `ticket/new` → `Screen.TicketCreate`, `customer/new` → `Screen.CustomerCreate`, `scan` → `Screen.Scanner`); new `resolveFcmRoute(intent)` consumes FCM `navigate_to` + `entity_id` extras (ticket/invoice/customer/lead/estimate/inventory → detail routes; appointment/expense/sms → list routes; unknown types → null). Both fire through `deepLinkBus.publish(route)` on cold start AND `onNewIntent` warm-start (which now also calls `setIntent(intent)` so any recomposition that re-reads `getIntent()` stays in sync). AppNavGraph collects `pendingRoute: StateFlow<String?>` via `LaunchedEffect`, dispatches `navController.navigate(mapped)` once, then calls `deepLinkBus.consume()` so configuration changes don't re-fire. Expanded `onNotificationClick` dispatcher in-app (notifications list tap) to match the same 9 entity types. `StateFlow<String?>` (not `SharedFlow` with replay=0) because the cold-start publish happens BEFORE the nav graph is composed and a replay=0 SharedFlow would drop that emission. Also added a small D5-1 spillover: annotated the decorative `contentDescription = null` sites in DashboardFab, SyncStatusBadge, OfflineBanner, MoreRowItem, MoreLogoutRow with inline comments explaining the sibling-Text labeling, and added `Modifier.semantics(mergeDescendants = true) { role = Role.Button }` on MoreRowItem + MoreLogoutRow so TalkBack collapses icon + label + chevron into a single focus item (helps D5-1 but doesn't close it — 60+ other sites remain). Commit 73bd971.

Result: **Clean — 60 packages audited, 0 suspicious.** No homoglyphs, no typo-squats, no low-reputation namespaces. Recorded methodology + full package list + result + recommendation as a new "Dependency typo-squat audit (PROD64, 2026-04-17)" subsection inside `SECURITY.md`'s existing "Supply-chain hygiene audits" section so future dep additions have a canonical diff-target. - [x] D5-5. `packages/android/app/src/main/java/com/bizarreelectronics/crm/ui/screens/pos/CheckoutScreen.kt` — two-part fix. **Snackbar spam:** the `LaunchedEffect(state.error)` error handler was re-keying on every `error → null → error` cycle (state-clear from `clearError()` followed by a fresh network-failure write), and `SnackbarHostState`'s FIFO queue forced the cashier to sit through 15 identical "Network error" toasts rotating off one at a time (~60s of dead UI on a broken Wi-Fi map). Primary debounce was already correctly wired before this task — `BrandPrimaryButton(enabled = state.canComplete && !state.isProcessing)` on the CTA + `if (s.isProcessing) return` in `completePayment()` — so the spam was purely from stale error states re-firing after each clear, not from unthrottled taps. Added belt-and-suspenders: `snackbarHostState.currentSnackbarData?.dismiss()` immediately before `showSnackbar(it)` so any in-flight toast is superseded rather than queued behind the new message. **Cash-vs-card offline split:** the pre-fix offline branch dispatched ALL `selectedMethod` values — including CARD — through `completePaymentOffline()` → `SyncQueueDao.insert("checkout", operation="convert_and_pay")`. `SyncManager.dispatchCheckoutEntry()` replays the entry once network returns by calling `ticketApi.convertToInvoice(...)` + `invoiceApi.recordPayment(...)`. That's correct for cash (funds are physically in the drawer, queue write is bookkeeping-only) but unrecoverable fraud exposure for card (no BlockChyp round-trip ever captured funds; the cashier could hand goods back on a "successful" local mark). Fix: added a method-discriminator in the offline branch — CARD surfaces error "Card payments require an internet connection. Switch to Cash to save offline." and flips `isProcessing=false` without queuing; CASH + OTHER continue to the existing `completePaymentOffline()` path unchanged, preserving the offline-cash-sale happy path through `SyncQueue` + `onSuccess()`. Verified with `./gradlew :app:compileDebugKotlin` — BUILD SUCCESSFUL. Commit aa7f23d.

- [x] D5-8. Walked every screen under `packages/android/app/src/main/java/com/bizarreelectronics/crm/ui/screens/` for the `OutlinedTextField` / `TextField` + missing-`Modifier.imePadding()` combination. 14 of 19 input-bearing screens already wired `imePadding()` at the Scaffold / outer Column from earlier work; the chat/SMS composer (`SmsThreadScreen.kt`) already had it. The five gaps were all detail screens whose bottom-anchored dialogs and inputs (payment-record amount, stock-adjust quantity, ticket comment composer, part-search price, profile password/PIN change) sat inside a Scaffold whose root `modifier` was unset — the soft keyboard ate them instead of the content resizing. Patched `TicketDetailScreen.kt`, `InvoiceDetailScreen.kt`, `ProfileScreen.kt`, `TicketDeviceEditScreen.kt`, and `InventoryDetailScreen.kt` by adding `modifier = Modifier.imePadding()` (with a `// D5-8:` comment per site explaining the specific inputs it protects) to each `Scaffold(` call. Four of the five files already imported `foundation.layout.*` with a wildcard so the symbol resolved for free; `TicketDeviceEditScreen.kt` used explicit per-symbol imports, so also added `import androidx.compose.foundation.layout.imePadding`. Paired with a manifest fix: `AndroidManifest.xml` `<activity android:name=".MainActivity">` gained `android:windowSoftInputMode="adjustResize"` — without it the system sometimes applies `adjustPan` (platform default on some OEM skins), which slides the whole Activity up blindly and defeats `imePadding()`. `adjustResize` is the mode Compose `imePadding` is designed against. Verified with `JAVA_HOME=...Android Studio/jbr ./gradlew.bat :app:compileDebugKotlin` — BUILD SUCCESSFUL (pre-existing deprecation warnings only, no new errors). `LoginScreen.kt` already had imePadding on its outer Box, `SmsThreadScreen.kt` / `SmsListScreen.kt` / `CustomerDetailScreen.kt` / every `*CreateScreen.kt` were already covered by prior work. - [x] SEC-M47. - [x] SEC-H35. `services/stripe.ts` `handleWebhookEvent` switch adds four cases: `charge.dispute.created` (logs loudly + resolves tenant via `stripe_customer_id` — no auto-downgrade since disputes are operator-response events), `charge.refunded` (audit-only log + tenant link so `stripe_webhook_events.tenant_id` is no longer NULL for refund deliveries), `payment_intent.payment_failed` (marks tenant `payment_past_due=1` via customer lookup; does NOT touch `failed_charge_count` because `invoice.payment_failed` is authoritative for dunning and Stripe often fires both), `customer.subscription.trial_will_end` (enqueues an email on the existing `stripe_payment_failure_emails` queue with `attempt_count=0` as the informational-marker; downstream worker can pick subject-line by attempt_count). All four fill `recordedTenantId` so the BL2 idempotency row gets the tenant_id backfilled. Commit da58685.

- [x] SEC-M57. `utils/validate.ts validateRequiredString()` now rejects control codepoints < U+0020 (except TAB/LF/CR) and RTL-override U+202A..U+202E / U+2066..U+2069 via new exported `rejectControlAndRTL()`. Closes log-injection (CR/LF in identifiers splits one log line into two) and presentation-spoofing (RTL flip renders 'TechStore' as 'erotSkceT' in UI lists). Exported helper lets other specific validators opt in. Commit d42dc13.

- [x] SEC-M21. `portal.routes.ts POST /register/send-code` adds a 24h hard cap of 10 codes per phone on top of the existing 3/hour hourly limit. Closes the slow-drip spam vector: 72 codes/day at 20-minute intervals. New rate_limits category `portal_send_code_day`. Over-cap returns 429 'Daily verification cap reached...'. CAPTCHA-on-first-new-IP renamed SEC-M21-captcha + deferred — requires CAPTCHA provider integration. Commit 6233747.

- [x] SEC-H38. Migration 104_gift_card_code_hash.sql adds `gift_cards.code_hash` + index; `services/giftCardCodeHashBackfill.ts` hashes legacy rows at boot (idempotent, per-tenant under multi-tenant). `giftCards.routes.ts` lookup now selects on `code_hash`, INSERT writes both plaintext (two-step rollover for existing redemption scripts) + hash, `generateCode` bumped 64→128 bits (`randomBytes(16)` = 32 hex chars). `audit_log.details` `code` field replaced with `code_prefix` (4 chars) + full `code_hash`. Plaintext code still returned on POST / ONCE for the cashier. Follow-up: drop the plaintext `code` column once all callers are hash-first. Commit 948be32.

- [x] SEC-H51. `POST /estimates/:id/convert` uses a conditional UPDATE as a lock: `UPDATE estimates SET status='converting' WHERE status NOT IN ('converted','cancelled','converting')`. `changes=1` → caller wins; `changes=0` → 409 "Estimate is already being converted. Try again in a moment." Final UPDATE at :760 flips 'converting' → 'converted'. Closes the two-convert race where concurrent clicks could produce two tickets + consume two tier slots from one estimate. Commit 3bb69d8.

- [x] SEC-H50. `POST /estimates/:id/approve` admin-override branch rejects with 403 when `req.user.id === estimate.created_by`. Previously any admin could approve their own estimate, bypassing two-party sign-off. Customer-token branch (where the approval comes from the email/SMS link, not a shop user) unaffected. SELECT grew `created_by` column. Commit f020495.

- [x] SEC-H49. `DELETE /tickets/:id` stock-restore cascade now only credits `ticket_device_parts` rows whose `status` is `'available'` / `'received'` / NULL (legacy). `'missing'` parts never decremented stock to begin with; `'ordered'` parts haven't arrived from the supplier — restoring either MINTS inventory. Theft primitive closed: a user who could soft-delete a ticket with missing lines can no longer inflate physical count. Cancel path (F5) already had this invariant; delete now matches. Commit 5d40ec1.

- [x] SEC-H48. `POST /invoices/bulk-action action='void'` now mirrors the stock-restore loop from the single `/:id/void` path (S7 / invoices.routes.ts:674) — iterates `invoice_line_items WHERE inventory_item_id IS NOT NULL`, credits `inventory_items.in_stock`, writes `stock_movements` audit rows with `reason='Invoice bulk-voided — stock restored'`. Prior bulk branch only flipped status + marked payments voided, permanently decrementing stock on every bulk-voided POS invoice. Either path now lands the shop in the same inventory state. Commit 887f95f.

- [x] SEC-H46. `PUT /repair-pricing/adjustments` tightened `pct` bound from `-100..1000` to `±50` (hard reject) with a `confirm_large_adjustment` gate for `20 < |pct| <= 50`. Prior wide bound let a fat-finger / compromised session 11x every repair price in one call. Normal ±20% band passes without friction; anything louder requires an explicit confirmation flag the UI can surface as a modal. Commit cf97ef7.

- [x] SEC-H44. `services/stripe.ts` `acquireCustomerLock()` now stamps `stripe_customer_lock_at` (epoch-ms, idempotent `ALTER TABLE tenants ADD COLUMN`) and steals stale locks older than `CUSTOMER_LOCK_TTL_MS = 60_000`. Prior 0/1 flag held forever on mid-acquire crash; every subsequent upgrade attempt 409'd until an operator ran a manual UPDATE. Release nulls both flag + timestamp. Happy path still sub-millisecond; TTL is crash-recovery backstop. Commit 9219854.

- [x] SEC-H37. Migration 103_currency_columns.sql adds `currency TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'USD'` to invoices, payments, refunds, gift_cards, deposits, pos_transactions. Indexed on the 3 tables most likely to get per-currency reports (invoices/payments/refunds). Single-currency tenants keep working — existing rows backfill to USD, new INSERTs without an explicit currency still succeed. Paired with SEC-H34-money-refactor (deferred) — when REAL→INTEGER cents lands, cents + currency will ship together so reports know which minor-unit denomination each row uses. Commit 46bcdf7.

- [x] SEC-H42. `blockchyp.routes.ts POST /process-payment` adds a 30-second dedup against `payment_idempotency WHERE status='completed' AND (invoice_id, amount) matches AND created_at > now()-30s`. Returns 409 with a cashier-readable "wait 30s and retry if intentional" when the window matches — BL7 idempotency_key only stopped SAME-key replays, not fresh-key retries from a frustrated cashier after a terminal timeout. IP binding intentionally skipped because CGNAT retries rotate src IP in seconds; invoice_id+amount is the authoritative pair. Commit a04d30b.

- [x] SEC-H43. `blockchyp.routes.ts POST /process-payment` now rejects with 403 when `req.user.role` is not admin/manager. Prior auth-only gate made a compromised cashier session a live-charge primitive (commits shop to settlement fees + refund path regardless of charge outcome). Matches the role gate already on gift-card issuance + refund creation + trade-in accept. Cash/check payments still go through the non-card POS path open to technicians. Commit 72c2b3a.

- [x] SEC-H39. `/pos/transaction` wraps the ticket INSERT in try/catch; on throw `refundTierReservation()` decrements `tenant_usage.tickets_created` by 1 (clamped at 0) so a failed INSERT doesn't permanently burn a free-tier slot. Covers the primary failure window (between reservation commit and first successful row write). Later per-device / invoice INSERTs don't refund because by then the tenant correctly owns a ticket. Best-effort — master DB errors during refund don't cascade. Commit e7c4678.

- [x] SEC-H36. `POST /invoices` line-item `tax_amount` now recomputed server-side from `tax_classes.rate` when the line item carries `tax_class_id` — matches `pos.routes.ts:413` canonical pattern. Prior code trusted client-supplied `tax_amount` so a hostile POS client could ship 0 and skip state collection. Legacy path (no tax_class_id) still accepts explicit tax_amount to keep pre-tax-class invoices working. Android offline flow intentionally unchanged per TODO note. Commit d489692.

- [x] SA2-1. `tickets.routes.ts` PUT `/:id` customer_id handling hardened: rejects non-number/string types with 400, coerces string → int, requires positive integer, writes normalised value back to req.body so the downstream UPDATE binds a primitive. Prior code forwarded object/array shapes directly into better-sqlite3 which surfaced as a 500 with a bind-error stack trace. Commit 633e6b4.

Five more primary CTAs migrated from raw `Button { }` to `BrandPrimaryButton { }` so the filled-orange hierarchy is consistent without per-site color overrides: CustomerDetailScreen "Create Ticket", InvoiceDetailScreen bottom-sticky "Record Payment", CheckoutScreen "Complete Payment" (dropped explicit containerColor), LeadDetailScreen "Convert to Ticket", TicketCreateScreen Step 4 "Continue to Details". - [x] SEC-H27. `tracking.routes.ts` — every public tracking route (`GET /track/:orderId`, `GET /track/portal/:orderId`, `GET /track/portal/:orderId/history`, `POST /track/portal/:orderId/message`, `GET /track/portal/:orderId/invoice`) now reads the tracking token via `extractTrackingToken(req)`, which prefers `Authorization: Bearer <token>` over the legacy `?token=` query parameter. Query-param hits still work during a 90-day deprecation window so old customer email links don't 404, but each one emits a `logger.warn('tracking token supplied via deprecated ?token query parameter', { route, method, user_agent })` so ops can watch client traffic migrate off the query path before the branch is removed (~2026-07-16). `GET /track/token/:token` is unchanged — its token sits in the URL path, not the query string, so it does not leak through access-log query patterns. Rationale: bearer-style credentials leaked in query strings end up in web-server access logs, browser history, HTTP Referer headers, and upstream proxy logs; Authorization headers do not. Commit bb51b95.

- [x] SEC-H32. `tracking.routes.ts POST /portal/:orderId/message` — added portal-session bypass on top of the existing tracking-token + 3/min IP rate limit. New `extractPortalSessionToken()` + `loadPortalSession()` helpers probe `portal_sessions` using the same credential shape as `portal.routes.ts portalAuth` (Authorization header OR portalToken cookie). If the session is valid AND (scope=full AND ticket.customer_id matches session.customer_id) OR (scope=ticket AND session.ticket_id matches the resolved ticket), the handler skips the tracking-token requirement AND the rate-limit bucket, and records `ticket_history.description = 'Customer left a message via authenticated portal session'` plus a `via: 'portal_session'` marker in the response. Anonymous/tracking-token callers keep the exact pre-fix behavior: 3 messages per minute per IP, tracking_token required, generic history description. Also touches `portal_sessions.last_used_at` when the session is used so portal idle-timeout (4h) stays in sync. Net: full-portal customers can reply without hitting the anti-abuse cap, bad actors are still throttled. Commit 63620f6.

- [x] SEC-M20. `management.routes.ts` — documented the per-handler tenantId validation invariant at the top of the file. All three mutating tenant endpoints (`POST /tenants/:slug/suspend`, `/activate`, `DELETE /tenants/:slug`) already: (a) accept the tenant id ONLY via URL path param `:slug`, (b) run `validateSlugParam` (rejects anything outside `^[a-z0-9]([a-z0-9-]*[a-z0-9])?$`, max 30 chars), (c) `SELECT id, status FROM tenants WHERE slug = ?` in master DB and 404 if not found, (d) route through canonical helpers in `services/tenant-provisioning.ts` (suspendTenant/activateTenant/deleteTenant) so pool close + plan cache bust + WebSocket disconnect + soft-delete grace all happen in one place, and (e) write `managementAudit()` rows with `tenant_id`, `previous_status`, and operator IP. No handler accepts a `tenantId` or `tenantSlug` from body/query. Super-admin JWT is enforced upstream by `managementAuth` (role + `super_admins.is_active = 1`). No code change — the invariant is codified in a docstring so future mutating endpoints follow the recipe. Commit 51afe9f.

- [x] PROD53. `utils/logger.ts buildEntry()` walks meta bag + masks PII by key hint in production at info/warn/error levels. Rules: `email` keys → `***@domain.tld`; `phone`/`to`/`from`/`mobile` (when value looks like a phone) → `***-***-NNNN`; `address`/`street` → `[REDACTED:address len=N]`. Walks one level into nested objects so webhook `{data:{to,from}}` payloads mask inside `data`. Debug level + non-prod keep raw values. Commit 461d81e.

- [x] PROD35. No `'*'` wildcard anywhere. `credentials: true` is spec-safe because the cors library reflects the specific origin on true-return. SEC-M52 already dropped LAN auto-accept in production. Verified.

- [x] DEBUG-SEC1. Bare-IP dev tenantResolver bypass hardened with a two-key gate: `NODE_ENV !== 'production'` AND `APP_ENV === 'development'`. Production sets only NODE_ENV; an operator would have to affirmatively set APP_ENV=development to re-enable the bypass — matches DEBUG-SEC1(b) intent. One-shot `log.warn` banner ("DEBUG-SEC1 active: bare-IPv4 Host headers routed to dev tenant. Must be off in production.") fires on first bare-IP request per process boot via `bareIpBypassBannerShown` module flag — DEBUG-SEC1(d). Trusted-proxy-only restriction (DEBUG-SEC1 c) intentionally skipped — dev needs to accept from any LAN IP; the double-gate is the more enforceable control. Also fixed bypass ordering (runs before isAllowedHostname) in commit 79a4e2e. Commit 4431d50.

- [x] PROD56. `services/retentionSweeper.ts` ROW_POLICIES audited. Sane defaults in place: automation_run_log 90d, webhook_delivery_failures 30d, rate_limits 1d, sms_retry_queue 14d, notification_retry_queue 30d, report_snapshots 365d, import_rate_limits 7d. Plus SEC-AL5 audit_logs 730d (separate cron). `cost_price_history` / `catalog_price_history` intentionally indefinite. Tiered 7d+4w+12m backup-file retention (spec's example) is a separate backup-file pruning concern; current `pruneBackups(dir, keep)` uses flat `backup_retention` config default 30. That's acceptable for the self-hosted single-shop use case; tiered S3-style retention is a future nice-to-have, not a correctness issue. Verified; no code change.

- [x] PROD47. Cross-tenant ID guessing — per-tenant DB isolation: the `tenantResolver` middleware (`index.ts:967`) swaps `req.db`/`req.asyncDb` to the per-tenant SQLite file based on Host subdomain before any handler runs. A ticket/invoice id from tenant A cannot surface on tenant B's subdomain because the SELECT runs against B's file. Same invariant already documented for payment_links in SEC-H33 — applies fleet-wide. Row-level `tenant_id` columns are only present on master DB tables (tenants, tenant_usage, billing); per-tenant tables don't need them. No code change; documented as verified.

Only `.db.enc` artifacts land under backup_path in production; encryptFile() already unlinks the plaintext input. Dev retains the opt-in behavior for engineer convenience. Commit 3ac65b4.

- [x] PROD54. `services/backup.ts:getPassphrase()` throws `BACKUP_ENCRYPTION_KEY is required in production. ... refusing to encrypt with JWT_SECRET fallback.` when `config.nodeEnv === 'production'` and the key is missing. Previously silently fell back to JWT_SECRET with a warn log → any JWT rotation bricked every backup. Dev retains the warning-only fallback so self-hosted test installs work without a dedicated key. - [x] PROD52. Correlation ID middleware in `index.ts` (mounted right after the HTTPS redirect, before helmet/cors) attaches `res.locals.requestId` and echoes `X-Request-Id` on every response. Prefers validated-incoming header `[A-Za-z0-9_.:+-]{1,128}` for cross-service log chaining; falls back to `crypto.randomUUID()`. Hostile incoming values with CRLF/log-separator chars rejected → fresh UUID. Enables "paste the reference from the user's error screen into the log aggregator" support flow. Commit eb4a9fe.

- [x] PROD29. New `utils/ssrfGuard.ts` exports `assertPublicUrl(url)` + `fetchWithSsrfGuard`. Blocks non-http(s) schemes + every resolved IP in private/reserved ranges (RFC 1918, 127/8, 169.254/16 inc. AWS IMDS, 100.64/10 CGNAT, multicast, reserved; IPv6 ::1, fc00::/7, fe80::/10, IPv4-mapped). DNS lookup requests ALL addresses and rejects if ANY is private → closes rebinding. Applied to `services/webhooks.ts attemptDelivery()` and `services/catalogScraper.ts fetchSearchPage()`. `githubUpdater.ts` uses child-process `git fetch` (no HTTP fetch; covered by origin-URL whitelist). Commits a5a3b56 + dd83f4d.

- [x] SEC-H20-partial. Super-admin JWT `expiresIn` shortened from `4h` to `30m` (`super-admin.routes.ts:19`). Full-fleet mutation blast radius too large for a 4h window — 30m aligns with PCI-DSS privileged-access guidance. Step-up TOTP on destructive endpoints (the remainder of SEC-H20) tracked as follow-up since it needs a UI prompt path. Commit b0ae99e.

- [x] SEC-M17. `tradeIns.routes.ts` PATCH `/:id` — accepting a trade-in now commits an inventory row and store credit atomically with the status flip. Previously the handler only updated `trade_ins` and left inventory + store credit to separate follow-up calls that could silently never run (or run twice, or run after a crash). New flow: pull existing `status, customer_id, device_name, condition, accepted_price` up front; detect the "was-not-accepted → is-now-accepted AND effective accepted_price > 0" transition, build a `TxQuery[]` batch containing (a) the UPDATE on trade_ins, (b) an INSERT into inventory_items (name=device_name, item_type='product', device_type='trade_in:<condition>', cost/retail=accepted_price, in_stock=1, is_active=1), (c) store_credits balance upsert (read-then-branch because 026_refunds_credits.sql has no UNIQUE(customer_id) — falls back to UPDATE if the row exists, INSERT if not), (d) store_credit_transactions ledger row (`type='manual_credit'`, `reference_type='trade_in'`, `reference_id=trade_in_id`, `notes='Trade-in credit'`). Inventory INSERT always runs on accept (simplest path); store credit only mints when customer_id is set (null customer_id is a valid state for walk-in / one-off trade-ins, ledger stays clean). Audit entry grows `accepted_transition` + `store_credit_issued` fields. Commit bdab160.

- [x] SEC-L18. `index.ts` — new per-tenant failure circuit wraps the tenant-retention-sweep (hourly→daily at 02:00 local) and appointment-reminder (every 15 min) cron handlers. One bad tenant (corrupt DB, schema drift, wedged SMS provider) used to burn CPU on every subsequent tick forever — the inner try/catch swallowed errors but the same doomed code path re-ran every tick. Added `cronCircuits: Map<string, {consecutiveFailures, openUntil}>` alongside the existing `cronLastRun` map, with helpers `circuitAllowsRun`, `recordCircuitFailure`, `recordCircuitSuccess` keyed on `(cronName, tenantSlug ?? 'default')`. After 5 consecutive failures the tenant is skipped for 10 minutes before retrying; any success clears the counter and the open window both. For appointment reminders, a per-message SMS failure does NOT count as a tenant-level failure (bad phone numbers and transient provider errors are bounded by design); only an uncaught tenant-work failure rolls up. Circuit state is in-memory per-process — cron jobs only run on one node so this is fine. Commit 4414d5c.

- [x] SEC-M43. `pos.routes.ts` `/checkout-with-ticket` — card-method overpayment now routes excess to store credit instead of silently dropping it. Previously `change = max(0, paid - total)` fired on every payment method, including card. On cash that's correct (hand back a bill); on card BlockChyp had charged the full amount but the invoice clamped amount_paid to total and the rest evaporated. New flow: card tenders (`card`, `credit`, `debit`, `blockchyp`, `stripe`) get their overpayment captured into `cardOverpayment`; in split-payment mode, cash tenders first cover the invoice total and only the card-method excess is store-credited (prevents mixed $50 cash + $100 card on a $90 invoice from losing the card excess). All payment inserts + POS transaction insert + store_credits upsert + store_credit_transactions ledger INSERT now build a `TxQuery[]` batch and run under one `adb.transaction()`. store_credits upsert uses the same read-then-branch pattern as SEC-M17. Ledger fields: `type='manual_credit'`, `reference_type='card_overpayment'`, `reference_id=invoice_id`, notes identifying the method. Response now exposes `store_credit_issued` so the UI can show the split instead of silently pocketing. Commit 1c0f73a.

- [x] SEC-M44. New migration `100_payment_capture_state.sql` adds a `capture_state TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'captured' CHECK (capture_state IN ('authorized','captured','voided'))` column to `payments` plus an index on that column. Backfills defensively (`UPDATE payments SET capture_state = 'captured' WHERE capture_state IS NULL`). `refunds.routes.ts` POST `/` now rejects with 400 when any payment on the target invoice has `capture_state != 'captured'` — blocks refunding money that was never captured (auth-only) or already released (voided). Error message names the count and the distinct non-captured states so the operator knows whether to capture or void first. Uses `COALESCE(capture_state, 'captured')` for defense-in-depth against any row that somehow escapes the backfill. `blockchyp.routes.ts` charge INSERT now writes `capture_state='captured'` explicitly since BlockChyp charges capture immediately on approval; making it explicit removes the silent dependency on the column default. Stripe INSERT sites: none currently exist server-side (Stripe flows today go through webhook paths that don't insert into payments); default 'captured' covers any future direct INSERTs. Commit 1fe0f60.

- [x] SEC-M51. `auth.routes.ts` TOTP encryption key derivation — v3 replaces raw `SHA-256(jwt+sa)` with HKDF-based (RFC 5869) derivation using `crypto.hkdfSync('sha256', Buffer.from(jwt+sa), Buffer.from('bizarre-totp-salt-v3'), Buffer.from('totp-key-v3'), 32)` and binds the version tag as AES-GCM AAD via `cipher.setAAD(Buffer.from('v3'))`. HKDF's extract/expand pattern gives a proper PRF with salt injection and `info`/IKM/salt domain separation; raw SHA-256 over a concatenated string provides none of that. AAD binding closes a theoretical downgrade-by-prefix-rewrite: tampering the version prefix on `v3:iv:tag:data` now fails the GCM auth tag (verified manually — rewriting v3→v4 fails with `Unsupported state or unable to authenticate data`). v1/v2 legacy keys stay in `ENCRYPTION_KEYS` for decrypt; `decryptSecret` only calls `setAAD` when `version >= 3` so all pre-existing ciphertexts continue to read unchanged. New encrypts route through `CURRENT_KEY_VERSION=3`. `super-admin.routes.ts:94,103` is still using the old `sha256(sa + ':totp:superadmin')` pattern — separate follow-up; out of scope for this commit. Commit e85a2e1.

- [x] SEC-H18. `middleware/auth.ts:185` `requirePermission()` evaluation order flipped: customRolePermissions now runs BEFORE the `users.role === 'admin'` bypass. Previously an admin assigned a narrow custom role via `PUT /roles/users/:userId/role` (which writes `user_custom_roles` only, not `users.role`) kept full permissions because the admin bypass short-circuited. Now the custom role is authoritative when assigned; legacy admin bypass still applies when no custom role is pinned (prevents org lockout). Commit 2a99b6b.

- [x] CROSS38b-notif. Android Settings > Notifications preferences sub-page. New `NotificationSettingsScreen.kt` (VM + Composable) wired via a new `Screen.NotificationSettings` route (`settings/notifications`). Six toggle rows split across two cards: Delivery channels (Email alerts / SMS alerts / Push notifications) and Categories (Low-stock / New-ticket / Appointment-reminder). Each backed by a new boolean on `AppPreferences` (`notifEmailAlertsEnabled`, `notifSmsAlertsEnabled`, `notifPushEnabled`, `notifLowStockEnabled`, `notifNewTicketEnabled`, `notifAppointmentReminderEnabled`) defaulting ON. `SettingsScreen` gains a new `onNotificationSettings: (() -> Unit)?` callback and renders a top-level "Notifications" `SettingsRow` using the same card-with-clickable-row shape as Edit Profile, sitting under SETTINGS. `AppNavGraph` registers the route, the SettingsScreen composable passes `onNotificationSettings = { navController.navigate(Screen.NotificationSettings.route) }`, and the NotificationSettings composable pops back on its own back button. Distinct from the notifications INBOX (`NotificationListScreen`) per CROSS54 — this configures which events fire; the inbox lists events that already fired.

- [x] PROD12. Migration 101_pin_set_flag.sql adds `users.pin_set INTEGER DEFAULT 0`. `/auth/switch-user` rejects with 403 + `code: 'PIN_NOT_SET'` when matched user's pin_set is 0 (still on provisioning default '1234'). `/auth/change-pin` flips pin_set → 1 on success. Mirrors password_set flow. Existing users forced to rotate on next switch — safer default than silently accepting 1234. Commit fceebbe.

- [x] PROD32. `index.ts` — HSTS header now only emitted in production via a `hstsConfig` constant (`config.nodeEnv === 'production' ? { maxAge: 15552000, includeSubDomains: true } : false`). Prior config sent `max-age=63072000; includeSubDomains; preload` unconditionally, which burned the self-signed dev cert into every local browser cache and required a manual `chrome://net-internals/#hsts` purge on a fresh checkout. 180-day max-age matches the TODO.md spec and gives operators a reasonable rotation window without locking clients out on a cert swap. `preload` intentionally omitted — hstspreload.org registration is a separate opt-in decision once the operator controls a real apex cert. Commit c145c7f.

- [x] PROD33. Audit of all 5 `res.cookie()` call sites in `packages/server/src`: `auth.routes.ts:271` (refreshToken on login), `:828` (deviceTrust), `:1024` (refresh rotation), `:1179` (impersonation), and `utils/csrf.ts:32` (portalCsrfToken). All had `HttpOnly` (except CSRF intentionally JS-readable for the double-submit pattern) and `SameSite` already set — but `Secure` was hardcoded `true`, which silently drops the cookie on any dev tooling that talks plain HTTP. Gated `Secure` on `config.nodeEnv === 'production'` on all five so prod still forces HTTPS-only cookies while dev over HTTP (test tablets / curl) gets a usable session. No change to HttpOnly/SameSite/path/maxAge semantics. Auth cookies keep `SameSite=strict`; CSRF keeps `SameSite=lax` + `httpOnly=false` per double-submit design. Commit f706cbf.

- [x] PROD34. `index.ts` helmet CSP audit — docs-only outcome, already tight. Global CSP: `default-src 'self'`, `script-src 'self' https://static.cloudflareinsights.com` (NO `'unsafe-inline'` in global CSP for prod OR dev — Vite HMR uses `<script src=>` + eventsource, not inline), `script-src-attr 'self'` (no inline onclick handlers), `frame-ancestors 'none'` globally with per-tenant allowlist on `/widget`. `style-src 'unsafe-inline'` retained intentionally — Tailwind runtime utilities and React-injected `<style>` tags require it; style-injection blast radius is far smaller than script injection. Documented exceptions: `/admin` and `/super-admin` HTML routes set a relaxed per-route CSP with script `'unsafe-inline'` for legacy inline onclick handlers in the backup panel — both routes are localhost-only, scoped override not a global relaxation. Added PROD34 block comment above global `helmet()` call and expanded comment on `adminCsp` constant so a future auditor doesn't re-derive what's tight vs. relaxed. Commit c3738a7.

- [x] PROD36. `index.ts:799-856` CORS config audit + harden. Prior inline origin callback mixed the no-origin fast path with the allowlist match, making it easy for a future refactor to accidentally short-circuit and reflect an unvetted origin while `credentials: true` is set (the classic CORS-spec violation). Extracted the match into `isCorsOriginAllowed(origin)` so the rule is: no Origin -> `callback(null, true)` (no ACAO emitted anyway, credentials moot); origin in allowedOrigins / BASE_DOMAIN + subdomains / LAN (dev only) -> reflect; anything else -> reject with `new Error('CORS not allowed')`. Added PROD36 comment block making explicit that credentials can only ride on a reflected explicit origin, never on `*`. No behavior change for legitimate clients; hardens against future refactor drift. Commit b2ca864.

- [x] PROD37. `ws/server.ts` WebSocket upgrade audit. Existing protections verified: `index.ts:670-685` `verifyClient` rejects bad Origin with 403 BEFORE socket accept (SEC-WS1, mirrors HTTP CORS allowlist); 5-second `authTimeoutHandle` terminates any socket that has not sent a valid `{type:'auth', token}` frame; invalid JWT closes with 1008 + clears timer; per-socket 60/min rate limit closes with 1008. Gap closed: an unauthenticated socket that sent a non-auth message used to log a warning, reply with an `error` frame, and leave the socket open for the full 5s window — a scanner could hold sockets open and burn fd + heap. Now `close(1008, 'not authenticated')` fires on the first non-auth inbound, shrinking the window from 5s to one message round-trip. Token-at-handshake (query param / subprotocol) kept out of scope — browser WebSocket constructor cannot set custom headers, and moving the check earlier would require concurrent web + Android client rewrites. Commit bb191b9.

- [x] CROSS9a. Ticket history section on Android `CustomerDetailScreen`. Added `CustomerApi.getTickets(id, page=1, pageSize=10)` hitting the existing server endpoint `GET /customers/:id/tickets` which returns `{ tickets: [TicketListItem], pagination }` — same shape as the main ticket list so `TicketListData` is reused without a new DTO. `CustomerDetailViewModel` fires a third parallel fetch (`ticketsJob`) alongside detail + analytics; null state = still loading or silent-degrade after fetch failure, empty list = loaded with no tickets. `CustomerDetailContent` picks up a new `recentTickets: List<TicketListItem>?` parameter and renders a `BrandCard` "Ticket history" section between the quick-stats row and the Call/SMS action row (matches the spec wording "under the quick-stats row"). Each row is `T-XXXXX (mono) · device name · BrandStatusBadge · $price`, tap routes to `TicketDetail` via the existing `onNavigateToTicket` callback. Max 10 rows enforced client-side via `.take(10)`. CROSS9 parent split into CROSS9a (done), CROSS9b-needs-api (notes — no server endpoint), CROSS9c (addresses), CROSS9d (tag chips).

- [x] SEC-H19. `startAutoClockoutSweep` in `employees.routes.ts:618` now iterates every active tenant DB in multi-tenant mode instead of running once against `config.dbPath` (which points at master in MT). Branches: MT → SELECT slugs from master + `getTenantDb(slug)` + `createAsyncDb(pooled.name)` per tenant; single-tenant preserved. Per-tenant errors log + skip so one broken DB doesn't block the rest. Before: every tenant's stale clock entries stayed open forever. Commit 70c0325.

- [x] SEC-H17. Migration 100_recovery_cooldown.sql adds `users.last_backup_recovery_at`. `/auth/recover-with-backup-code` stamps the column on success. `PUT /settings/users/:id` now rejects role changes with 403 for 24h after the target's last recovery (`Role cannot be changed for Nh after a backup-code recovery`). Closes the vector where an attacker with a stolen backup code + leaked email could run recovery and immediately escalate / demote other admins before the real user notices. Password/PIN change within the window still allowed. Commit 8d90bfc.

- [x] NEW-TLIST-GRP. Android ticket list rows now render a small group pill to the LEFT of the specific status badge so the high-level bucket is scannable at a glance. Added private `TicketStatusGroup` enum + `ticketStatusGroupFor(TicketEntity)` mapper to `TicketListScreen.kt` with inference rules: `statusIsClosed && !looksCancelled → Complete (green)`, `name contains cancel/void → Cancelled (grey)`, `name contains waiting → Waiting (tertiary/amber)`, else `In Progress (primary/orange)`. Rendered as a compact `Surface` pill (`surfaceVariant` bg + single-hue label text) matching the `BrandStatusBadge` visual weight, with a 6dp spacer between the group pill and the specific status badge. Non-breaking for the existing trailing-column layout (pill + badge live in a nested `Row`, the money line stays on the second line). Because `TicketEntity` does not carry a dedicated `is_cancelled` column (only `statusIsClosed`), cancellation is inferred from the status-name heuristic — same style the spec already allowed for the Waiting group.

- [x] SEC-H33. Payment-link public routes verified as DB-level tenant-isolated: `payment_links` has no `tenant_id` column because the architecture uses a per-tenant SQLite file. Global `tenantResolver` middleware (`index.ts:967`) rewrites `req.asyncDb` to the per-tenant DB based on Host subdomain, so a token minted in tenant A's file cannot be found via tenant B's Host. - [x] NEW-MSG-EMPTYHINT. Android Messages empty-state subtext updated from "Tap the edit icon to start a new conversation" to "Tap the + button to start a new conversation" at `SmsListScreen.kt:262`. Post-CROSS42 the new-conversation action is a FAB (pencil/plus) at bottom-right, so the prior wording pointed users at a non-existent edit icon in the top bar.

- [x] SEC-H24. `tracking.routes.ts:77` `toPublicTicket()` no longer includes `tracking_token` in the unauth `/track/:orderId` response. Token is a 32-char random bearer credential — returning it in a public lookup let any probe with a valid order_id harvest the token and reuse it on other portal paths to impersonate the customer. Authenticated `/customers/:id/tickets` still returns it (role-gated). SMS-OTP-gated reveal remains future work. Commit e4fc965.

- [x] SEC-M60. `paymentLinks.routes.ts` — `/:token/click` and `/:token/pay` now reject with 410 Gone when `expires_at` is in the past. Prior code only enforced `status = 'active'` which left active-but-stale rows replayable until someone hit GET (which is the only handler that auto-flipped `status` to `'expired'`). Both mutation endpoints now SELECT `expires_at` alongside the row, flip to `'expired'` when the check fires, and throw `new AppError('Payment link has expired', 410)`. Portal UI can read 410 as "permanently unavailable — ask shop for a new link" instead of treating it like a transient failure.

- [x] SEC-M45. Portal `portalAuth` middleware now enforces a 4-hour idle timeout on top of the existing 24-hour absolute `expires_at`. Pulls `last_used_at` on lookup; if stale, DELETEs the session row and returns 401 `Session idle timeout. Please log in again.` Active users (who touch `last_used_at` every request) never kicked. Closes the shared-workstation resume-as-previous-customer vector. CSRF synchronizer-token migration out of scope this pass — separate work. Commit c1f8dc9.

- [x] SEC-M59. `estimates.routes.ts:893-926` — NULL `approval_token_expires_at` no longer means "never expires". Previously the expiry branch was gated on truthy check which silently skipped enforcement for legacy rows signed before the expiry-policy migration, leaving leaked pre-policy links replayable indefinitely. Now the code explicitly rejects with 410 Gone (`"Estimate approval token has no expiry — signed before expiry policy rolled out; ask shop to reissue"`) so the shop has to reissue the estimate. The 410 status (vs 403) tells email clients / portal UI the resource is permanently unavailable so UX can render a clear "ask for a fresh link" message instead of looking like a generic auth failure.

- [x] SEC-M50. `db/tenant-pool.ts:104` — no code change. `busy_timeout = 5000` was already correct. Added a rationale comment documenting the choice: multiple crons (session cleanup, payment-idempotency janitor, retention sweeps, appointment reminder) race on the same tenant DB when tick intervals overlap, and the 5s window serializes writers instead of letting SQLite return `SQLITE_BUSY` immediately. 5s covers normal DELETE / WAL checkpoint + safety, short enough that a genuinely stuck writer is surfaced rather than papered over for minutes. Raising this would mask real deadlocks; lowering causes flaky retention runs on busy tenants.

- [x] SEC-M54. `/estimates/bulk-convert` now refunds unused quota slots via `UPDATE tenant_usage SET tickets_created = MAX(0, tickets_created - failCount)` after the conversion loop. Prior flow atomically reserved `estimateCount` up-front and kept every slot even if mid-loop failures (not-found / already-converted) left fewer real tickets created — permanent over-charge against monthly plan limit. Best-effort refund: master DB failures log without throwing, so the user's mixed-result response isn't replaced by a 500. Runs only on multi-tenant + finite tier. Commit b9c0db7.

- [x] SEC-M49. `index.ts` — new daily per-tenant DB size observability cron. Fires once per UTC day during hour 02 (between the 02:00 tenant-timezone retention sweeps and the 03:00 master retention sweep), guarded by `shouldRunDaily('tenant-db-size-monitor', 'UTC')` so it runs exactly once even if the hourly interval lands multiple times in the window. Per tenant, it reads `tenantDb.name` (the better-sqlite3 file path), calls `fs.statSync(dbFile).size`, and emits one `log.info('tenant db size', { slug, sizeBytes, sizeMB })`. No archival, no delete — that belongs to SEC-AL5 (audit logs) and the retention sweeper respectively. One syscall per tenant per day, negligible budget. Ops can chart DB growth over time and catch a runaway tenant before it stalls the whole node on a full disk.

- [x] SEC-M46. New `deleteStripeCustomer(id)` helper exported from `services/stripe.ts` (returns false if Stripe not configured, idempotent on 404). `archiveDueTenants()` in `services/tenant-provisioning.ts:615` promoted to async and now best-effort-deletes the Stripe customer when `tenants.stripe_customer_id` is set before flipping status to 'deleted'. Failures log warn and archive proceeds — dead tenant shouldn't hang on Stripe 5xx. Closes PII-retention gap on archive. Commit fa72b3c.

- [x] CROSS50-header-needs-api. Quick-stats row under the customer avatar now renders ticket count, lifetime value, and last-visit relative time. `CustomerDto.kt` gains a `CustomerAnalytics` data class matching the server's `{ total_tickets, lifetime_value, avg_ticket_value, first_visit, last_visit, days_since_last_visit }` payload; `CustomerApi.getAnalytics(id)` hits `GET /customers/:id/analytics`. `CustomerDetailViewModel` constructor-injects `CustomerApi` and fires `loadAnalytics()` in parallel with `loadCustomer()` — a separate `analyticsJob` cancel/relaunch so `loadCustomer()` can retry independently. UiState gains a nullable `analytics: CustomerAnalytics?`; a failed fetch leaves it null and the row silently doesn't render. `CustomerDetailContent` picks up a new `analytics` parameter and (when non-null) renders a three-column `Row(Arrangement.SpaceEvenly)` with `QuickStat` children: Tickets (count), Lifetime ($N whole dollars), Last visit (`DateFormatter.formatRelative` on the ISO string). Analytics row sits between the avatar and the Call/SMS button row so the detail starts with STATE then ACTION. No DTO schema migration needed on the Android side — the analytics response is a parallel fetch, not an addition to `CustomerDetail`. Commit 5c280e9.

- [x] CROSS47-wizard-avatar. Ticket wizard customer-search results now render the shared `CustomerAvatar` initial-circle composable (`ui/components/shared/CustomerAvatar.kt`) as their leading content instead of the generic `Icons.Default.Person` glyph — same visual treatment as `CustomerListRow` and `GlobalSearchScreen` customer hits. `TicketCreateScreen.kt` picker list's `ListItem.leadingContent` swaps out the `Icon(Person)` for `CustomerAvatar(name = buildCustomerName(customer))`. Pure render change; no state / wiring / DTO changes. Commit bef06d4.

- [x] CROSS52. Customer Edit form top-bar duplicate Save removed — the bottom sticky Cancel+Save row is the single thumb-reach save target (`CustomerDetailScreen.kt:239-257`, comments call out the CROSS52 split). Introduced by commit 7df49d4. Sweep check on other edit forms: `InventoryEditScreen.kt` has only the top-bar Save (no duplicate) and `TicketDeviceEditScreen.kt` follows the same pattern; nothing to strip. The "sweep" portion of the original TODO turned out to be a non-finding — customer edit was the only offender — so closing the tracker.

- [x] CROSS53. Customer Edit Group field already using the shared `OutlinedTextField` shape (label floats inside the border outline, read-only + Clear trailing icon) — matches every other field in the edit form (`CustomerDetailScreen.kt:437-451`). Introduced by commit 7878edd. No further code change needed; closing the TODO tracker.

- [x] CROSS56. Customer Edit Tags placeholder already switched from developer-placeholder `"tag1, tag2, tag3"` to tenant-relevant `"VIP, corporate, loyalty"` (`CustomerDetailScreen.kt:460`). Introduced by commit 3b86f9b. The autocomplete-from-existing-tenant-tags follow-on is still future work but the immediate "looks like leftover placeholder" UX bug is closed.

- [x] SEC-M56. `sms.routes.ts` — two-part hardening. (1) Per-destination rate limit: before inserting the outbound row we call `consumeWindowRate(req.db, 'sms_per_destination', convPhone, 3, 3600_000)` so at most 3 messages/hour can be sent to the same normalized phone number. Keyed on `convPhone` so "+15551234567" and "(555) 123-4567" hit the same counter. Prevents buggy integrations / template-render loops from hammering one customer with dozens of messages in a few minutes. (2) Phone redaction in logs: new `redactPhone()` helper masks the carrier prefix and keeps only last 4 (`XXX-XXX-4567`). Applied to `logger.warn('outbound sms not delivered', { to, ... })` -> `{ toRedacted, ... }` and `logger.info('sms auto-reply sent off-hours', { from })` -> `{ fromRedacted }`. Customer phone numbers no longer land unredacted in the ops log aggregator / shared dashboard.

- [x] SEC-M58. `services/dunningScheduler.ts:408` `cutoffDateIso()` now takes a `timeZone` param; callsite reads `store_config.store_timezone` via new `getTenantTimezone()` helper. Uses `Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-CA', { timeZone })` for clean YYYY-MM-DD in tenant zone. Prior UTC cutoff produced 7h early/late drift on non-UTC tenants around DST, causing embarrassing 11 PM SMS sends. No new deps. Commit 6e9268c.

- [x] SEC-M55. `sms.routes.ts:414-440` — POST `/sms/send` now enforces a per-tenant daily outbound cap in addition to the existing 5/min per-user window limiter. Before inserting the outbound row we run `SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sms_messages WHERE direction='outbound' AND status NOT IN ('failed','simulated') AND created_at > datetime('now','-1 day')` and throw a 429 once the count hits `DAILY_TENANT_SMS_CAP` (default 500, override via env `TENANT_SMS_DAILY_CAP`). `'sending'` and `'scheduled'` rows are included in the count so in-flight messages debit the ceiling and a burst cannot race past the limit before statuses settle. Carrier-fraud containment: bounds a compromised tenant / stolen API token to at most 500 messages/day instead of 7200 (what the 5/min limiter allows at steady drip).

- [x] SEC-M41. Migration 099 adds `user_id` column to `payment_idempotency` + new `UNIQUE(invoice_id, client_request_id, user_id)`. `blockchyp.routes.ts:178` lookup + reserve INSERT now include `req.user!.id`. Prior narrow UNIQUE let a stolen `(invoice_id, idempotency_key)` pair replay from another user's session and leak original charge's transaction_id/amount via the 'replayed' happy path. Existing rows backfilled from `invoices.created_by`. Commit 8e727cd.

- [x] SEC-M52. `index.ts:792-817` production CORS no longer auto-accepts RFC1918 / CGNAT / localhost origins. The LAN / loopback regex now runs only when `config.nodeEnv !== 'production'` so prod is narrowed to `ALLOWED_ORIGINS` + `BASE_DOMAIN` (+ subdomains). Dev retains the permissive rule so shop tablets can hit the server by LAN IP during testing. If an operator wants to whitelist a LAN origin in prod they must add it explicitly to `ALLOWED_ORIGINS` in the env. Closes the browser-extension / shared-host spoof path where a malicious neighbor on the LAN forges an `Origin: http://192.168.x.x` to bypass CORS against the public API.

- [x] SEC-M37. `inventory.routes.ts:1680` quick-add now runs `cost_price` / `retail_price` through `validatePrice()` (400 on non-finite / negative); empty/undefined still defaults to 0 for the convenience flow. `repairPricing.routes.ts:45-46` gains a local `safeNum()` wrapping `parseFloat` + `Number.isFinite` check when reading `repair_price_flat_adjustment` / `repair_price_pct_adjustment` from `store_config` so bad rows can't turn into Infinity in downstream arithmetic. Commit ad7cc2e.

- [x] CROSS47-seed. Android ticket wizard now accepts and pre-seeds customerId from a nav arg. `Screen.TicketCreate` gained a `createRoute(customerId: Long? = null)` builder and the composable is registered with an optional `customerId` query arg. `TicketCreateViewModel` injects `SavedStateHandle`, reads the arg on init, and a new `setPickedCustomer(id)` helper resolves the row via `CustomerRepository.getCustomer(id).filterNotNull().firstOrNull()` then populates `UiState.selectedCustomer` and advances to the Category step — same end-state as tapping a search result. Idempotent: if the user already picked a customer (or walk-in) between launch and the flow completing, the seeder no-ops. Bottom-nav visibility check updated from `== Screen.TicketCreate.route` to `.startsWith(...)` since the registered route template now carries the `?customerId={customerId}` suffix. CustomerDetail's onCreateTicket callback now calls `createRoute(customerId)`. Commit d46d70e.

Purely a duplicate-link removal — the top-level row already routes to ProfileScreen. - [x] CROSS16-ext. Nine list screens that were missing bottom inset padding now carry `contentPadding = PaddingValues(..., bottom = 80.dp)` so the last row clears the bottom-nav / gesture area. - [x] CROSS22-badge-cap. - [x] SEC-M62. `DELETE /tickets/:id` now gated on `requirePermission('tickets.delete')` and hard-blocks when the associated invoice has any `amount_paid > 0`. Prior route was auth-only so any logged-in user could cascade-delete tickets, triggering stock restores and invoice voids. Paid-invoice delete is now rejected regardless of the allow-delete-after-invoice toggle — the admin must refund first so the revenue event is debited, not erased. Commit a56e7bb.

- [x] SEC-L39. Recurring appointment auto-generation (`leads.routes.ts:477`) now uses `addMonthsClamped()` that pivots to day-1 before `setMonth` and clamps to the target month's last valid day. Prior `setMonth(getMonth()+i)` silently rolled Jan 31 → Mar 3 on non-leap years (and April 31 → May 1). Weekly/biweekly unchanged — `setDate()` already exact across DST for the server's TZ. date-fns not pulled in (would be a new dep) — native Date is sufficient for this clamp. Commit 6ede85a.

- [x] SEC-L23. `services/stripe.ts` exports `resetStripeClient()` that sets the module-level `stripeClient` back to null. Any super-admin path that rotates STRIPE_SECRET_KEY at runtime can now call this helper; the next `getStripe()` lazy-inits a fresh client with the new key. Previously the singleton was cached for process lifetime so a rotated key was silently ignored until restart. Commit 761a1ae.

- [x] SEC-L27. Portal `widget.js` now validates `data-server` against a CNAME pattern `https://<sub>.<domain>.<tld>[:port][/path]` (dev exemption for localhost / 127.0.0.1). Prior code accepted any string, so a malicious embedder could point the widget at an attacker-controlled origin and render a lookalike portal to phish customer credentials. Commit a89ff84.

- [x] SEC-L44. 2FA backup codes switched from 32-char hex to 16-char Crockford base32 formatted `XXXX-XXXX-XXXX-XXXX` in `auth.routes.ts:780`. Crockford alphabet (0-9 A-Z minus I L O U) excludes confusable pairs so users typing codes off paper don't fat-finger 0/O or 1/l/I. 80 bits of entropy — still well above NIST's 10^-6 guess-rate bar for 8 single-use codes. Verify path unchanged (bcrypt.compareSync is format-agnostic); already-enrolled users keep working. Absorbed into commit d46d70e via concurrent-session git interleave (wrong commit message — real content change is the Crockford swap in `auth.routes.ts:776-800`).

- [x] SEC-L40. `invoices.routes.ts` payment_plan validator now cross-checks `installments * amount_per ≈ invoice.total` with tolerance `$0.01 + installments * $0.01` for penny-split rounding. Prior checks validated each field in isolation so 6 × $10 on a $100 invoice could be saved. Mismatch rejects with 400 and a message showing both sums. Commit fb325aa.

- [x] SEC-L38. Boot-time `import_runs` zombie recovery added to `index.ts` (runs alongside the SMS sweep after `migrateAllTenants()`). Per-tenant UPDATE marks any `import_runs.status IN ('running', 'pending')` as `failed` with `error_log` entry tagged `zombie-recovery: import crashed / server restarted before completion`. Also DELETEs stale `import_locks` rows so new imports can start. Commit b6562fa.

- [x] SEC-L42. `/signup` validation errors — malformed email, invalid-format slug, slug-already-taken — now all return one generic `Signup failed. Please check your details and try again.` instead of three distinct strings. Prior differences let probes enumerate taken slugs (AZ-042). Validation still runs; specific reason flows to `logger.warn` for operator debugging, never to the wire. Per-email rate limit 429 message unchanged. Commit cf6e581.

- [x] SEC-L29. `paymentLinks.routes.ts` public-route token validators (GET /:token, POST /:token/click, POST /:token/pay) now check `^[A-Za-z0-9_-]{32}$` — matching the 24-byte/32-char base64url output of `generateToken()` exactly. Prior `length >= 8` guard let 62^8-space garbage reach the DB lookup. Commit 1d0a0cb.

- [x] CROSS45-ext. `BrandWaveDivider` (`ui/components/WaveDivider.kt`) was pulling its hairline color from `MaterialTheme.colorScheme.tertiary`. CROSS45 unified placement; CROSS45-ext makes the decorative flourish independent of theme — the wave is the one sanctioned magenta moment per `project_brand_accent.md` and must stay `#BC398F` regardless of any future primary/tertiary change. Replaced `val magenta = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.tertiary` with a file-local `private val WaveMagenta = Color(0xFFBC398F)`. Docstring now spells out the color policy: primary CTAs route through `colorScheme.primary` (orange); the wave is the ONLY place the codebase hardcodes magenta. Confirmed no other screen uses `tertiary` as a semantic primary (`SharedComponents.StatusTone.Magenta`, `SyncStatusBadge` tertiaryContainer, `LeadDetailScreen` StatusTone.Magenta are all decorative/status-tone). Commit 4d5bc28.

- [x] CROSS15. `TicketCreateScreen.kt` step 2 label renamed from "Category" to "Device Type". Audit of `CATEGORY_TILES` (line 99) confirmed the tiles are device-kinds (Mobile / Tablet / Laptop-Mac / TV / Desktop / Game Console / Other), NOT repair categories — so step order is correct (device-type-before-model filters the model picker) and only the user-visible label was wrong. Changed `TicketCreateStep.CATEGORY` enum-constant's `label` from "Category" → "Device Type" and the CategoryStep screen heading "Select Category" → "Select Device Type". Enum constant kept as `CATEGORY` to avoid churn across ~15 call sites in nav / back-stack / goToStep plumbing; only the user-facing string moved.
